Current Affairs Commentary

A Delicate Stage of Diplomacy 44

— Hua

At a time when bandit-puppet troops were launching their second fierce attack on Bailing Temple; at a time when over two thousand Japanese troops had landed in Qingdao, searching party headquarters and arresting many people; suddenly, new developments occurred in the diplomatic arena in Nanjing. According to a Central News Agency dispatch from Tokyo on the 4th, "The sudden meeting between Foreign Minister Zhang and Ambassador Kawagoe on the evening of the 3rd, and the lengthy statement issued by the Japanese Embassy in Nanjing, have caused considerable surprise here." This so-called "surprise" is bound to be puzzling to many who have not seen this lengthy statement. However, based on the facts, we can understand the origins of the "surprise" to some extent. According to a Reuters dispatch from Nanjing, during the talks on the evening of the 3rd, Ambassador Kawagoe presented Foreign Minister Zhang with a document said to be a summary of the past seven talks. However, this record did not match the facts of the talks. Foreign Minister Zhang asked Kawagoe to take it back, but Kawagoe refused. Foreign Minister Zhang then had someone return it to the Japanese Embassy. The embassy sent it back again, and our Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent it back again. During this period, the Japanese Embassy issued the so-called diplomatic statement. Following this, Ambassador Kawagoe left Nanjing for Shanghai on the 5th. Because of this scene of comedic back-and-forth, rumors spread that the negotiations had failed. At the same time, political circles in Tokyo expressed extreme "surprise."

Why the surprise? Was it due to the dispute over this document? Yes, but not entirely. Was it out of concern that the negotiations would be interrupted? Yes, but not entirely either. We believe that the biggest reason for the other party's surprise is that we have stood firm and will not allow any further retreat. Hundreds of millions of Chinese people are watching the content of the past seven negotiations. This is not something that can be confused with a piece of paper. Hundreds of millions of Chinese people have firmly stood behind the brave men of Suiyuan Province. We are not worried about the interruption of negotiations. In this way, the diplomats who felt things were easy during the Tanggu and Hebei negotiations suddenly encountered a tricky experience. This is probably the reason for the surprise in Tokyo's political circles.

However, in practical terms, the current stage of Sino-Japanese diplomacy has indeed reached a very delicate stage. We cannot but pay close attention to and prepare for this situation. Regarding the progress of the negotiations, according to news from Tokyo and the statements of Ambassador Kawagoe, there is no intention to give up. However, in future negotiations, will this so-called lengthy statement be used as a basis? What the people of China are currently concerned about is that the negotiations must proceed on an equal footing and not allow unilateral oppression. Our position should be to recover lost sovereignty first and not allow any further loss of sovereignty. Does the other party have a full understanding of these two principles?

Naturally, we, the people, are bound to be quite surprised by this so-called lengthy statement. What is even more surprising is that while diplomatic negotiations are underway, the same opposing side has planes and tanks attacking Bailing Temple, and large numbers of troops from the same opposing side have invaded our Qingdao. What a surprising way to conduct diplomacy!

However, amidst the surprise, we are not afraid, because the millions of soldiers and civilians of our country have stood very firm and cannot retreat any further.

French Foreign Minister Announces Foreign Policy: Should England and Belgium be Invaded, Military Assistance Will Be Decisive 45

(Paris) The Chamber of Deputies began discussing foreign policy this afternoon. Foreign Minister Delbos delivered a speech, the main points of which were: "I hereby declare on behalf of the French government that if England and Belgium are invaded without provocation, France will immediately provide the full military force of its naval, land, and air forces to defend England and Belgium." As for the "fire" within Spain, France has made every effort to extinguish it, preventing it from spreading. The purpose of this is solely for the sake of the overall European situation. Referring to the general European situation, he said that the rapprochement between France and Germany is necessary to maintain peace in Europe. "We ask ourselves, we do not want to dominate Europe, nor do we want to encircle Germany. Therefore, the rapprochement between France and Germany is not impossible. The mutual assistance pact between France and Russia has no aggressive nature, and any other country can join." At this point, Delbos reiterated the Spanish issue and elaborated on the Communist Party's advocacy for France to restore free trade with Spain, saying that the majority of the French people support the government's current policy of non-interference. "I personally sympathize with the Spanish Republic, but I am in charge of diplomacy and bear the great responsibility of war and peace, so I cannot be swayed by emotions. Those who demand that the government cancel the non-interference agreement, once they seize power, their actions will not be any different." Subsequently, right-wing member Renault spoke, saying that France should be militarily closer to the Soviet Union, but this is impossible while the People's Front government is in power, because French public opinion is wary of the current government's excessive sympathy for the Third International. Therefore, "only a government that is completely unaffected by the Communist Party can promote close cooperation between the French and Russian general staffs." The Chamber of Deputies then adjourned, and decided to continue the meeting tomorrow, at which time two motions will be proposed to end the debate: one is a motion on the policy of non-interference in the Spanish Civil War, and the other is a vote of confidence in the government. It is expected that the Communist Party will abstain from voting on the first motion and will vote in favor of the second motion. (4th Havas Dispatch)

(London) Government officials are very satisfied with the foreign policy speech delivered by French Foreign Minister Delbos in the French Chamber of Deputies yesterday, believing that it is an automatic response to Foreign Secretary Eden's previous speech in Leamington, and it is also of great benefit to clarifying the relationship between England, France, and Belgium. In addition, the cooperation between England, France, and Belgium does not want to exclude other countries, which will increase the difficulty of negotiating the new Locarno Pact. (5th Havas Dispatch)

Brussels French Foreign Minister Delbos said in his speech in the Chamber of Deputies yesterday, "If England and Belgium are invaded by other countries without provocation, France will immediately provide full military assistance." Government officials here have expressed their satisfaction, believing that Belgium's policy of complete independence does not hinder the friendship between France and Belgium, which can be clearly demonstrated here. (5th Havas Dispatch)

Therefore, the act of amending the Covenant is unlikely to achieve practical results. Pope's Ailing Leg 51

(Rome) Pope Pius XI, suffering from edema, has a swollen leg and is extremely uncomfortable. He was unable to conduct prayer services at the Vatican this morning, and, following doctors' orders, canceled all scheduled events. It is reported that the Pope is in good spirits and met with Secretary of Ecclesiastical Affairs Archbishop Basili this morning, and then approved several documents. All Vatican affairs are proceeding as usual. So far, no one has prayed for the Pope's recovery in the chapel. The Pope, who is 79 years old, is the first reformer among the Popes, and the installation of modern scientific inventions in Vatican City began with him. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

Vatican City Pope Pius XI, who is old and unwell, has a worsening case of gout. His left leg is no longer movable. He was unable to attend Mass as usual this morning, which is a cause for great concern. Attending physician Amintore Milani has asked him to rest and recuperate. Well-informed sources have also said that the Pope is now only able to conduct affairs in his private study, sitting in an armchair. (5th Havas Dispatch)

Japan's Military Industry is Developed 52

(Tokyo) The Ministry of Commerce and Industry had been investigating the number of factories, employees, and production value in each prefecture nationwide in the Showa 10th fiscal year. This time, excluding the six prefectures of Tokyo, Osaka, Kyoto, Kanagawa, Gifu, and Shimane, the investigation of the remaining forty prefectures has been completed. On the 5th, the summary statistics of the forty prefectures and the comparison with the previous year were announced for the first time. According to the results of the investigation, at the end of December in Showa 10, the total number of factories in the forty prefectures was 50,298, an increase of 2,795 factories compared to the previous year. The number of employees was 1,488,867, an increase of 125,150 compared to the previous year. In terms of production value, it was 6.002537893 billion yen, an increase of 771.997583 million yen compared to the previous year, indicating that military demand is booming nationwide. (5th Allied Dispatch)

Mrs. Simpson Arrives in France and Travels South: Where She Will Stop is a Mystery of the Situation. She Called the British King by Telephone En Route 53

Blois, France Mrs. Simpson continued her journey by car from here today. It is said that she is going to Piarrritz. Mrs. Simpson stopped briefly yesterday due to the cold and fog, and took the opportunity to call the British King by wireless telephone. (5th Nationalist Dispatch)

Roanne, France Mrs. Simpson drove through here by car this morning, heading for the Riviera coast in the south. (5th Havas Dispatch)

Cannes, Southern France Mrs. Simpson's luggage, after her arrival in France, was transported here this morning. (5th Havas Dispatch)

(Paris) Mrs. Simpson flew from England to Ivry-les-Tilleuls in France yesterday on the British King's private plane. After having lunch at a hotel, she called London and then continued by car, with plainclothes detectives as escorts. Her destination is strictly kept secret. Her whereabouts have been reported to the world. (5th Reuters)

(Paris) Mrs. Simpson arrived in France with two confidants of the British King today and hurriedly traveled south. It is said that she is going to Cannes to visit her American friends Mr. and Mrs. Rogers. Her car passed through Troyes at 4:03 PM today, passed through Chatillon at 5:00 PM, and arrived in Orléans forty minutes later. However, when a United Press reporter spoke to Rogers by telephone today, Rogers denied that Mrs. Simpson was going there. (4th Nationalist Dispatch)

Orléans Mrs. Simpson arrived in France yesterday evening from Newhaven, England, landing at Dieppe, bringing a car. She passed through here this morning, heading for Blois. She stopped briefly at Evreux at noon and dined at the Grand Cerf Hotel. She was accompanied by a middle-aged man with graying temples. After the meal, Mrs. Simpson called London by long-distance telephone, and then left by car. (4th Havas Dispatch)

Blois Mrs. Simpson arrived here from Orléans by car at 8:00 PM yesterday and went to a hotel to rest. She resumed her journey at 3:20 AM this morning, destination unknown. (5th Havas Dispatch)

(London) General commentary on Mrs. Simpson's departure from England is that Mrs. Simpson's intention is to allow the King to freely change his mind. Great ladies often wait until the storm is over before returning to London. Unseen in Fourteen Years: Heavy Snowstorm in Various Areas of Jiangbei 61

Telegraph and Telephone Communications Completely Cut Off; Trains Delayed, Ships Sunk in Dalian Waters

Dalian Dispatch: On November 27th, the heavy snowfall in various parts of the Northeast reached nearly two feet. It has been fourteen years since the major snowfall of January 30, 1922. Such a heavy snowstorm can be described as unprecedented in all these years and has now become a disaster. Moreover, under the harsh rule of the Japanese puppet regime, the disaster-stricken people are crying out for food, and resentment is brewing. This is indeed a major hidden danger for the Japanese puppet regime. The details of the heavy snowstorm disasters in various parts of Northeast China are recorded as follows:

Telegraph and Telephone Lines Severed

Within the Guandong Leased Territory, except for the telephone service within Lushun city, all submarine cables, communication facilities, etc., between Dalian and Sasebo, and between Dalian and Changchun, have been completely cut off. In addition, wireless communications are also disrupted because the control line between the Liushutun relay station and the Dalian Central Telegraph Bureau is completely destroyed, resulting in a complete breakdown of communication. Telegraph and telephone lines from Dalian to the entire Northeast region are also completely out of service.

Trains on Various Lines Delayed

Due to the damage caused by the heavy snow, the situation on various railway lines in the Northeast is severely affected. (1) The downward bound No. 15 express train on the Lianjing Line (from Dalian to Changchun) was delayed and stopped at Pulandian, unable to depart. The downward bound Nos. 19 and 23 trains collided, resulting in several passenger deaths and injuries. (2) The upward bound train on the Anfeng Line (from Andong to Shenyang) stopped at Sujiatun. There are many other disaster situations on various lines that cannot be fully investigated and understood at this time.

Disaster in Dalian Waters

Due to the heavy snowstorm, land and sea transportation connections in the Liaodong Peninsula area belonging to the Dalian coast have been cut off. In addition, a total of 25 ships have been wrecked and sunk, including 4 motorboats, 1 small steamboat, and 20 sailing boats. The total loss in Dalian Bay is estimated to exceed 500,000 yuan.

After receiving instructions in person, he immediately returned to Suzhou and appointed Prosecutor Weng Zhuonian to handle the case. At 5:00 p.m. on the 4th, Shen Junru and the other six were escorted from the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau to Suzhou and directly to the High Court. Prosecutor Weng took the bench in the Eighth Tribunal and interrogated them separately for about two hours. He then ordered them to be sent to the High Court Detention Center on Heng Street, Wuxian County. At that time, Prosecutor Weng and Prison Officer Hui Hong, leading all the bailiffs, escorted the six prisoners to the detention center. That night, they were held in Wards 3, 4, and 5 of the center's infirmary. These wards were well-lit, spacious, and well-ventilated. There was also a lawn in front where they could take walks at will, which was quite comfortable and accommodating. Ward No. 1 was set aside as a dining room and a place for relatives and friends to visit. However, when relatives and friends visited, Prison Officer Jiang had to report to Prosecutor Weng at any time. Visits were allowed twice a day, in the morning and afternoon. Because Shen Junru has many relatives, friends, and students in Suzhou, there are many people who come to visit him. It is also heard that Prosecutor Weng will conduct on-site interrogation inside the detention center within days.

War Zone Correspondence (1) 63

At 10:04 a.m. on the 29th, our group of seven embarked on the PingSui Railway journey. The Yenching University Suiyuan Anti-Japanese War Relief Association, during a two-day suspension of classes, had students hand-making ten thousand hygiene kits, which were also being transported with us to the front lines.

In the third-class carriage, the passengers were unusually crowded. Everyone was bundled up in thick clothing, and standing on tiptoe in the crowd, they felt a bit sweaty. However, the conductor gave us unexpected preferential treatment, allowing us to move to the first-class carriage. During the 19-hour journey, we did not suffer the hardships we had anticipated. We felt ashamed and uneasy, but the conductor's kindness was deeply appreciated.

At 5:00 a.m. on the 30th, we arrived safely in GuiSui. Stepping onto this glorious land that has attracted worldwide attention, our hearts were filled with excitement and joy. At 9:00 a.m., we visited the provincial government to inform the authorities that the students of the Journalism Department of Yenching University had organized a war zone investigation team to introduce the situation in the war zone, which the people of the country were eagerly awaiting. At the same time, we brought the sincere admiration of eight hundred students for the loyal and brave soldiers who were defending the country here.

The militia in Suiyuan are very well-trained. This is a strong grassroots force, and this strength was bravely demonstrated in the anti-Japanese war in HongGeltu. Soon, we plan to visit the militia training center at Xiaoxiao Field to see what their training content and methods are.

This place is very quiet. The people all have calm faces. People coming from afar would hardly believe that there is an anti-Japanese war going on at the border.

After BaiLing Temple was captured, everyone was talking animatedly, and comfort telegrams and gifts came from all sides, almost overwhelming them. Therefore, a Joint Military-Civilian Association was specially established under the General Command for Bandit Suppression to manage these matters and to receive visiting well-wishers.

We are staying at the Dabeilv Hotel, which was recommended by the Provincial Government's Reception Office. It is said that this hotel used to be exclusively for foreign friends, and the owner was the owner of the famous Matsuda Mansion. Today, the gates of the Matsuda Mansion are tightly closed, locked with an iron chain. Mr. Matsuda, who used to be responsible for consular affairs and regularly transported military supplies to BaiLing Temple, has quietly disappeared. The owner of the Yushan Mansion, which served as a special agency, is still in Suiyuan, but his car no longer dashes and rushes on the streets, crushing small lives on the roadside as casually as stepping on an ant, and then dusting off his sleeves and leaving. Currently, there are only six foreign friends in the entire GuiSui city, but they are all very polite and have lost the kind of boisterous enthusiasm they used to have at the Suiyuan Hotel, such as firing guns for fun after getting drunk.

Today, we sent three students to BaiLing Temple with the Central Photography Team to investigate. Regarding that aspect, we will have a detailed report to present to the people of the whole country, who are rejoicing over this great victory.

In the morning, the four of us who stayed in GuiSui were led by Committee Member Qiao of the Joint Military-Civilian Association to two hospitals of the 35th Army to comfort the wounded soldiers. One place was on Xiaodong Street, where most of the soldiers were wounded in HongGeltu, a total of 58. They were all in good spirits. The lightly wounded only said that they would go to the front lines again as soon as they recovered. The other place was the Fourth Elementary School on Shangshanzi Street, which was considered a primary field hospital, housing 33 wounded soldiers, all of whom had participated in the attack on BaiLing Temple. Here we talked a lot with a Major Medical Officer Yun, who promised that we would come back and talk to the wounded brothers individually after returning from BaiLing Temple.

There are currently more than 120 wounded soldiers in GuiSui, and some are staying in public hospitals. This field hospital was only organized and established on the 11th of last month. The food and daily life of the wounded soldiers are very good. They eat 1.4 catties of foreign flour, 4 liang of millet, and 10 cents of vegetables every day, and they have meat with every meal. The wards have stoves and are very warm, and the bedding is very clean.

The morale in this anti-Japanese war is very high. All the lightly wounded refused to be carried on stretchers and refused to come down. They believed that as long as they had a breath left, they would never want to lose the opportunity to kill the enemy. This burgeoning enthusiasm greatly moved the officers, who all said that this was a situation that had never occurred since the 35th Army began fighting. Naturally, it is impossible to compare a national war with a civil war. How could a civil war make the people of the country excited and give them enthusiastic material and spiritual assistance?

Because of this loyal and brave anti-Japanese war, we have an even stronger belief in the future of the revival of the Chinese nation. (Meng Jue, sent from GuiSui, December 1)

Wu Jiang 64

Business Circles Enthusiastically Raise Funds to Aid Suiyuan

The Comfort Suiyuan Soldiers and Suppress Bandits Committee of all circles in this county resolved yesterday to set the minimum standards for fundraising in each district: 2,000 yuan for District 2, 3,000 yuan for District 3, 1,500 yuan for District 4, 3,000 yuan for District 5, 1,500 yuan for District 6, 800 yuan for District 7, and 1,000 yuan for District 8. Tao Changhua, Yang Xuemen, Gao Hongkui, Pan Xiangjun, Wang Youting, Zheng Fufu, and others were appointed to guide the fundraising in each district on December 4th. 446.72 yuan was raised in the urban area. In addition, the First District Office and the County Party Department are responsible for raising special donations from households in the urban area. The County Chamber of Commerce first initiated a one-day campaign in the urban area, donating 5% of business income. All agencies donated one day's income to aid this Suiyuan donation. All circles in Muxian County are very enthusiastic.

Song Jiang 66

Suspicious Persons Found in Hotel

The winter defense of this county has already begun. Military police inspect the hotels in the city and suburbs every night. On the fourth night, the military police of the Second Garrison found two suspicious men and women in the Heiyu Dafang Hotel. The man spoke with a Nantong accent and claimed to be Zhang Jinkui, an intelligence officer from the Fengxian Public Security Bureau. A symbol, a pistol, and nine bullets were found on him. When asked if he had official documents to come to Songjiang and the serial number of the pistol and the number of bullets, he was unable to answer. The woman, Sheng Yuefang, was 19 years old and said she was his mistress. The police considered them to be very suspicious and took them to the police station for interrogation.

Wuxi 67

Banks Accepting Copper Currency Notes

After the Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce convened a general meeting of members last month, it submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance based on the resolutions regarding the issue of exchanging old copper currency notes for national currency. The request asked the Central Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Three Banks to accept as many as possible, and requested the China Farmers Bank and the Zhejiang Local Bank to quickly establish exchange offices in Wuxi. After receiving the report, the Ministry of Finance has ordered all banks to comply and informed the Xishang Association.

Winter Defense Conference Held

The Wuxi County Government, due to the frequent burglaries and robberies in the city and countryside in the past half month, urgently needed to organize joint defense to maintain public security. Yesterday, it specially convened a winter defense conference with the water and land public security authorities, the security brigade, and the district chiefs of various districts. The resolutions are as follows: (1) A joint winter defense office will be organized immediately, with the county chief as the director, the public security chief and the security brigade deputy as the deputy directors, and the staff members of the first section of the county government and the inspectors of the public security bureau will be transferred to serve there. (2) Each autonomous region will organize a joint defense office separately by the district chief. (3) The joint defense office will be headed by the district chief. (4) The areas bordering the county public security sub-bureaus and branches of the four, five, six, seven, eight, and nine districts will regularly hold joint patrols with the Wujin, Cheng, and Su counties. (5) The strong men's teams, the public security sub-bureaus and branches, and the security teams will jointly undertake the tasks. (5) The mountain security teams will dispatch troops to strictly defend the important places within the county.

Collection of Donation for Airplanes for Birthday Celebrations

The Second District Special Commissioner's Office recently received an order from the province stating that many counties have not paid the donation for purchasing airplanes for birthday celebrations. It ordered that the donations be quickly collected and used to close the matter. It also ordered that county officials be selected to go to the counties to collect. The commissioner, upon receiving the order, specially appointed Zhang Zhongyu, the deputy chief of the district, to go to Wuxi, Wuxian, and Wujiang counties to collect the donations. Staff member Wang Zipei was sent to Changshu, Taicang, and Kunshan counties to collect the donations, and Jing Tian was sent to Wujin and Jiangyin counties to check the collections.

Chang Zhou 68

Robbery Case at Yuantong Nunnery Solved

The Yuantong Nunnery in the Fifth District of Wu County was robbed on the night of the 29th of last month. After Zhiwen, the abbess of the nunnery, escaped, she saw two robbers, Zhang Jinkun and Zhang Shanrong, whom she knew well, on a bright moonlit night. Afterwards, she immediately reported to the county government for their arrest. County Chief Hou immediately dispatched Detective Chen Sendu of the Detective Team to investigate and handle the matter. Chen and others went to the countryside early in the morning on the 3rd of this month and arrested Zhang Yukun and the other two. They did not admit the robbery. It was later found out that Zhang Shanrong's father, Zhang Churong, had colluded with the already executed bandit Yu Jinxi to rob the houses of Shan Yan Liu Chanlin and others in the Third District in January of the 23rd year. He had been wanted ever since. Detective Chen immediately took the two criminals to the city and handed them over to the county for interrogation in April.

Yang Zhou 69

Director of Rehabilitation Center Dies Tragically

Zhu Hanqing, Director of the Rehabilitation Center of the Jiangdu County Relief Institute, was targeted by the residents for filing a joint complaint with the Civil Affairs Department. The Tobacco Prohibition Committee investigated and sent Zhu to the Tobacco Prohibition Institute. It was found that he was old and weak and it would be difficult to quit. Zhu was already sick, and this ordeal worsened his condition. Yesterday (the 3rd), he was on the verge of death, and was only then released for medical treatment. He had just arrived home when he died. It is said that Zhu's wife is also seriously ill, and she was in critical condition after crying over his death. Zhu has three daughters who are not only saddened by their father's death, but have also lost their source of livelihood and feel hopeless. It is also heard that the institute has appointed Qin Wulou to succeed Zhu in managing the affairs of the institute.

Hang Zhou 70

Zhang Taiyan to be Buried in West Lake

Mr. Zhang Taiyan of Yuhang passed away in Suzhou this summer. The central government has issued a commendation order. However, Zhang's ancestral property was confiscated by the Political Affairs Committee in April of the 16th year of the Republic of China and ordered to be investigated by Yuhang County. In order to honor the local sage, the provincial government specially changed the name of the Qiaoxi Central Elementary School, built with 3,600 yuan of Zhang's confiscated private property, to Taiyan Central Elementary School to commemorate him. As for Zhang's tomb site, the Central Executive Committee, together with Zhang's family, has surveyed and determined Zhongtai Mountain in the outskirts of Hangzhou City as the burial site.

Zhejiang-Jiangxi Passenger-Freight Train Derails

The 12th passenger-freight mixed train on the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway, departing from Yushan to Jiangbian with 18 cars, derailed the fourth freight car at the 40-kilometer mark between the Meichi and Zhibu stations at 2:00 a.m. on the 4th, causing the cars behind it to also derail. The line was temporarily blocked. The passenger and freight trains going up and down that day were slightly delayed. On the morning of the 5th, the tracks were completely repaired and the trains were running normally. The derailed and overturned cars contained a large amount of goods such as paper, stones, tung oil, eggs, and cattle. It is said that other than the eggs being damaged, only the cattle were slightly injured. The more than 30 passengers were fortunate not to be injured, but were only frightened.

Commercial News

Yarn Flower: Reported Warehouse Yarn Stocks Only 500 Bales; Auction Yarn Sets New Price; Recently Auctioned at 268 Yuan; Spot Yarn Sales Rise Again by About 4 Yuan; Ewo Yarn Sold at 253 Yuan 71

The yarn market continues to advance, with a very strong momentum, mainly because of the lack of spot yarn, which causes panic among short sellers. The current selling price of Jincheng spot yarn has reached 280 yuan. It is said that the yarn stock in the yarn and cloth warehouse is only 500 bales, resulting in a new price for the January-February term yarn of 268 yuan. In the afternoon, it was reported that Ewo Factory released 800 bales of 20-count Five Blessings/Shepherd yarn at a price of 253 yuan. It was also said that the Qingdao Yarn Factory had news of resuming production. As a result, the short sellers covered their positions, and Changfeng also shipped out a large number of cases, so the market turned from high to flat.

Auction Yarn Becomes Even Tighter Recently

At the opening of the auction yarn market, prices rose across the board because spot yarn is extremely tight and the yarn stock in the warehouse is decreasing day by day, reportedly with only 500 bales remaining. As a result, short sellers were even more panicked, and new entrants were all wary. The market rose step by step. Near-month contracts jumped by 3 yuan at the third session, and the December term reached a new price of 268 yuan. The January term also reached 56 yuan. All terms rose above the new high price of the second day. Subsequently, Changfeng shipped a large number of cases at the third session, and the counter eased until the close of trading, and the market fell back. As a result, each term rose by 1.5 to 2.5 yuan compared with the close of the previous day. At the opening in the afternoon, it was heard that the spot yarn situation was still tight, and prices rose again by 2 yuan to 2.8 yuan, with the July term rising by 79 corners. Near-month contracts were still firm in the second session, while far-month contracts fell by 5 corners to 1.1 yuan. Until the third close of trading, the market slackened slightly due to the selling pressure from long sellers, with the current month falling back by 2.5 yuan and the far month falling by 67 corners. As a result, each term compared with the morning close of trading, with the January term rising by 3 corners and the far month falling by 4.9 corners. The sales were: Changchangfeng 11,800 bales, Ruidai 1,350 bales, Chengji 2,150 bales, Gengfeng 5,750 bales, Senkang 3,350 bales, Changyu 1,000 bales, Dachangcheng 1,650 bales, Taichang 2,200 bales, Yichang 1,150 bales, Tonghe 1,200 bales, Xincheng 2,200 bales, Runkang 2,950 bales. Purchases were: Hexing 3,000 bales, Juxing 1,000 bales, Dafu 2,200 bales, Yudai 5,000 bales, Dafeng 1,650 bales, Jinchang 1,300 bales, Xingchang 1,450 bales, Fengtai 1,750 bales, Yuanyi 3,150 bales, Shengyuan 5,850 bales. Cotton Prices Rise Slowly; Some Short Sales Have Been Hedged 72

Cotton prices rose slightly because the yarn market is doing well and rising step by step, and people are excited. Also, some cotton merchants are going long recently, slightly pulling up the price. However, the overseas Indian and American cotton markets are flat and lackluster, and the prices are too high, so the factory demand is not strong. But it is said that the Qingdao Yarn Factory has news of resuming production.

Auction Cotton Purely Driven Up by Term Yarn

At the opening of the auction cotton market, the prices rose uniformly, mainly because the yarn market is constantly reaching new peaks, and people are being carried away by it. Recently, some people who buy yarn and sell cotton have hedged their positions, buying back cotton and selling yarn. Therefore, the cotton market has been driven up, but new long positions are still rare. As a result, the prices of each term of auction cotton rose by 3.5 to 6.5 corners compared with the closing price of the previous day. The overseas cotton market is still bleak and weak. At the opening in the afternoon, it was reported that the Qingdao Yarn Factory had news of resuming production, and the yarn market was still firm, trending up by 1.5 to 2 corners. After the first session, it was heard that spot cotton trading was not smooth, and it fell into a state of fatigue again. As a result, the prices of each term fell by 5 minutes to 1.5 corners compared with the morning closing price. The sales were: Hexing 12,700 dan, Yudai 2,900 dan, Juxing 3,700 dan, Dafeng 3,300 dan, Gengfeng 5,500 dan, Changyu 1,100 dan, Wang Taixing 2,200 dan, Dachangcheng 9,600 dan, Taichang 6,000 dan, Yichang 3,700 dan, Changfeng 3,000 dan. American Cotton Reaches 2 Minutes of an Angle; Buyers Can't Help but Be Wary 74

American cotton opened yesterday with mixed prices, with small fluctuations. The prices of each month rose by 2 pound tones. Early in the morning, the market was slightly weak due to the release of 15 delivery notices, the liquidation of long positions in the December term, and short selling. Traders were the only buyers. Although the government report this month did not have any important changes, traders are still waiting. The mood in the market is biased towards the buying side due to rising prices of various commodities and firm spot prices. However, due to the instability of the political situation abroad, buyers cannot help but be wary when the price is above 2 minutes of an angle. At the close of trading, the market was slightly weak due to the liquidation of long positions. Spot prices were unchanged, and futures prices rose by 1 pound tone to falling by 8 pound tones. English cotton spot prices were unchanged, and futures prices rose by 12 points. Special Feature Reply to the Inquiry from the Economic Research Institute of Nankai University 75

Our institute plans to continue producing transaction indices for important Chinese commodities, and urgently needs your newspaper to publish market prices and transaction volumes of silk and tea to serve as references. However, we do not know the source of this data and the unit conversion methods (e.g., how many catties equal one case), whether it is futures or spot goods. We respectfully request your guidance and will be immensely grateful. This matter concerns academic research, and we hope for your favorable consideration. Please promptly investigate and reply. With utmost respect, initiated by the Economic Research Institute of Nankai University, Tianjin Private University (1st)

Regarding your inquiries, we have forwarded your letter to the Tea Firms Guild and silk investigators in this city. We now have the following responses:

The Tea Firms Guild stated in their letter: "Upon investigation, the weight of tea cases cannot be uniformly determined. Cases vary in size, and tea leaves also vary in weight. However, on average, each case weighs approximately fifty catties. If Nankai University desires detailed quantities, please inform them that they can directly inquire with our guild, and we will be happy to answer."

The silk investigators stated in their letter: "Raw silk is measured in bales, and there are no strict regulations regarding its weight. However, generally, it is around one dan (approximately 100 catties). (Some are less than 100 catties, while others exceed 100 catties, but the difference is not significant.) However, market prices are quoted per 100 catties of raw silk. Furthermore, all statistical figures for raw silk bales are also around one dan in weight, without precise catty figures."

In summary, although the above silk and tea are not for immediate delivery, they are of a spot nature. Moreover, our newspaper publishes monthly export inspection reports from the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, which include quantities in kilograms that are accurate and reliable and can assist academic research. This is for your information. No further correspondence will be sent. The Editor (5th)

Three-Brand Yarn Falls, While Futures Cotton Rises 77

On the 5th, according to a large Shanghai telegram, first-grade futures yarn fell by $1.20 to an increase of $0.10, with the near month at $243.50 and the far month at $200.18. Futures cotton rose by $0.30 to $0.50, with the near month at $67.10 and the far month at $68.35.

Grains: Wheat Prices Cannot Ease Without Firm Orders for Foreign Wheat 78

Yesterday, the wheat market was generally very firm for all months. Because the domestic wheat market had already fallen, if people want to calm down, they must make firm orders for foreign wheat, no matter what. Only then can general speculators let go. Therefore, although there were few transactions in the morning, the market still rose by 2.4.5 points. When the market opened in the afternoon, buying interest was strong again, and all months continued to rise by 3.5 points. The furthest term, such as April, reached a high of $7.02. Later, due to rumors of orders for foreign wheat, the market saw a pullback, falling by 35 points from the initial price. Currently, the wheat market is not active due to low arrivals. Customers are very concerned about the goods stored in Shanghai, and all factories are sticking to their supplies.

Flour Prices Have Risen Every Day This Month 79

Yesterday, the flour market rose uniformly again. Foreign wheat prices were slightly up by a dime in Chicago, up by four cents in Canada, and Liverpool rebounded by 12 pence. Therefore, when prices were set at the customs gate, outside buyers felt that foreign wheat was not suitable for ordering, and their courage seemed to grow stronger. On the domestic front, there are few statistics on the amount of wheat in storage, so general speculators were able to raise prices at will. Compared to the previous day, prices rose by 3.4.5 points for the near term and 1.2 points for the far term. When the market opened in the afternoon, outside bulls bought in large quantities again, and the prices for this month and January both rose by about 2 points. Transactions for February and beyond were also very active. However, some speculators also sold off in large quantities, and rumors of orders for foreign wheat led to a gradual stabilization of the market, falling back by 2.3 points from the highest price. As a result, the near term rose by 3.4 points, while March and April had minor fluctuations of half a point.

Hakka Xian Rice Merchants Eager to Sell – The Trade Still Stable 80

Yesterday, the Hakka Xian rice market was lackluster. However, inventories in the market gradually increased, and merchants were mostly showing samples to sell, so the market appeared soft and lifeless. But yesterday, the local street demand was still active, and some outside hoarders also stepped in. The Henan and Shantou gangs each took several hundred bags, so market prices remained stable. Only the Guangdong gang has suspended operations for days, and the merchants' minds are inevitably shaken. Therefore, while Fenmai and Hebei rice, as well as soybean oil and miscellaneous grains, are soaring, Hakka Xian has failed to rise. Throughout the day, more than 3,000 bags of Jiangxi rice, 1,320 bags of Hunan rice, 500 bags of Jiangbei rice, and 320 bags of Wenzhou rice were offered, with the prices similar to the previous market, and most of it was handled by local merchants.

River Rice Market Still Feels Stable 81

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, the sources from various gangs were similar to the previous day, with more than 80 firms still arriving, totaling more than 16,000 stones of goods. Among them, Bo Dao accounted for more than 50 firms. The local street sales were still acceptable. The Xunwei, Pingqingyan and other gangs handled more than 6,000 bags of Bo Dao and 1,4500 bags of Hou Geng. Therefore, although the prices of Hou Geng and Bo Geng have not seen much rise or fall, they have presented a situation of "tight on the surface, tight underneath". Du Yangjian is similar, with Yin Yuan stable.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, there were no arrivals from the west section of the Suzhou River, only two or three firms coming through the roundabout. Since the rice boats detained by Jiading County, the boats stored on the river have been scarce. Although the market is weak, customers are quite firm. Therefore, the price of Bai Geng was stable in the early market and turned tighter by several points in the afternoon. The price of Yangjian rose by 45 points, and the prices of Budu and Kejian also showed improvement. The price of early rice followed closely, while the price of Bo Dao was peaceful, and Yin Biang Yuan had no rise or fall. It is expected that the prices of other goods will rise in the future.

Silk and Tea: American Firms Sell 100 Bales of Silk 82

Recently, the overseas silk market has weakened. Yesterday, both Japan and the United States saw a slight rebound. New York standard silk futures each rose by 3.5 points. Japanese silk 83 and 75 saw a modest rebound of 2 points on average. However, Shanghai silk and Guangdong silk continued to fall by 2 points each in the United States. Yokohama spot prices fell by 5 yen, while futures rose by 8 yen. Lyon Shanghai silk AB grades both opened at the original price. Japanese silk and Guangdong silk each fell by one franc. The Shanghai silk market is still quite sluggish. American firms are selling silk, and Indian firms are still busy with sporadic transactions. Although the number is not large, the business situation this week is considered good. Domestic silk still shows no improvement, with only occasional transactions.

Piece Goods: Cotton Cloth Continues to Rise; Qingdao Goods Disappear Due to Strike; Fine Cloth and Fine Twill Rise Another 10-20 Cents 83

Yesterday, the cotton cloth market was still affected by the Qingdao strike, with no arrivals. The northern route had a large demand, which made the market even stronger. Raw materials and yarn, which are closely related, are seeing new high prices every day, and the rising tide lifts all boats, causing cotton cloth to rise even faster, initially unaffected by actual sales. Fine twill and fine cloth from Qingdao are usually plentiful, so yesterday the market rose another 10 to 20 cents. Coarse cloth, coarse twill, and flannel prices were all stable. Single-yarn woven goods such as Zhigong and serge, as well as flannel, are seeing prices for 42-count yarn soar to nearly 400 yuan, so each factory's supplies continue to increase by 1.5 to 1 cent per yard. Other non-seasonal goods such as poplin and bleached cloth from distant Guangdong, Sichuan, and Hunan were searched for and purchased in nearly 100 pieces, all of which were leftover goods from this year, and the selling prices are gradually increasing. There are still several batches under negotiation. Customer demand varies in urgency. Most believe that the price increase is too steep and the base is too high, fearing a backlash, so they are hesitant to act. In recent days, shipments have been scarce, and goods from the important cloth-producing areas of Wuxi and Changzhou have been cut off for three days due to poor waterway conditions, making the market feel even more lacking in spot goods.

Ordinary Colored Zhigong Woolen Fabric is Out of Stock 84

Huang Fu is Critically Ill 98

Has Entered a Moribund State

Huang Fu's condition became more serious from yesterday morning and has entered a moribund state. Traditional Chinese medicine practitioner Fan Shisheng and Western medicine practitioner O'Harley were still invited to diagnose and treat him, hoping to save him in the event of an emergency. Foreign Minister Zhang Qun and the newly appointed Chairman of Hubei Province Huang Shaoheng visited him in the morning. Both of them looked worried when they left. As of 12:00 p.m. last night, Huang's condition had not changed.

Preparatory Committee for the National Goods Joint-Venture Company, Wang Xiaolai and Others Returned to Shanghai 99

The National Goods Promotion Association Seeks Opinions

The National Goods United Business Company held an inaugural meeting of the Preparatory Committee in Beijing on the 4th. Wang Xiaolai, Liu Hongsheng, Qian Xinzhi, Huang Yanpei, and others from the city, who attended the preparatory committee, left Beijing that night and returned to Shanghai yesterday morning. Hu Xiyuan, Li Xinpu, and others returned to Shanghai yesterday afternoon. According to Li, this time, representatives from more than fifty factories, including household industrial societies, went to Beijing to petition the Ministry of Industry to expand the organization of the National Goods Joint Business Company in order to popularize it. After meeting Minister Wu Dingchang, the results of the presentation were very satisfactory. The company has now started a public offering of shares.

The Citizens' National Goods Promotion Association, in order to assist the government in preparing to form the China National Goods United Business Company, is seeking opinions from manufacturers. Yesterday, it sent a letter to all member manufacturers, saying that it had received a public letter No. 281 from the General Association of the National Economic Construction Movement Committee, which stated that "the application from your association to assist in widely establishing national goods companies has been approved. The committee is organizing the preparatory office of the China National Goods United Business Co., Ltd., which is jointly operated by the government and the business community, in order to promote the sales of industrial products. Participation and cooperation from other national goods organizations are also welcome. If you have any opinions, please suggest them to the Shanghai branch office," etc., and attached a copy of the preparation outline and the articles of association of the preparatory committee. After the meeting, it was decided to recommend Chen Yiting and Gan Tinghui to attend the preparatory meeting of the association, and report the preparation situation to the association for verification. The original letter, outline and articles of association of the National Economic Construction Movement Committee are hereby sent to your factory for reference. If your factory has any opinions, this association will forward them to the association for verification.

Duan Qirui's Funeral: Yesterday's Family Ceremony, Colleagues Paid Public Tribute Yesterday, Public Tribute from All Walks of Life Today, Moving the Coffin Tomorrow 100

Former Interim Executive Duan Qirui passed away in Shanghai on November 2. Yesterday, the family paid tribute, and colleagues from the funeral committee paid public tribute. It is scheduled to hold a tribute today, with public tribute from all walks of life, and move the coffin north tomorrow. The details are recorded as follows:

Men Arrives in Shanghai

Men Zhizhong, member of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council and chairman of the Construction Committee, came south to pay tribute to Duan Qirui on the order of Song Zheyuan, chairman of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council. He arrived in Shanghai by Shanghai-Ping through train at 7:50 a.m. yesterday and stayed at the Dadong Hotel. Then, at about 2:30 p.m., he went to Duan's residence on Avenue Joffre with Li Guanghan, Song Zheyuan's representative in Shanghai, to pay tribute. According to Men, the situation in Suiyuan is tense, but the situation in Peiping and Tianjin is still peaceful. Chairman Song is determined to protect the territory completely. If bandits invade, he will give them a severe blow. He has no other task other than paying tribute to Duan. He is scheduled to leave Shanghai for Tianjin on the 7th to meet Duan's coffin and return it to Peiping.

Family Ceremony in the Morning

The family ceremony was held at 10:00 a.m. yesterday. First, the son in mourning attire inscribed the tablet, followed by the family ceremony, and finally the guests and funeral committee members paid their respects.

Public Tribute in the Afternoon

At 4:00 p.m. yesterday, the funeral committee members held a public tribute, presided over by Gong Xinzhan. Because most of the funeral committee members were former subordinates, they performed the kneeling ceremony. In addition, those who went to pay tribute yesterday included Men Zhizhong and Li Guanghan, representatives of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council, Jiao Yitang, President of the Supreme Court, Xiang Hanping, representative of Guangdong Pacification Director Yu Hanmou, Deng Gang, representative of Guangdong Provincial Government Chairman Huang Musong, Zhang Fang, member of the Henan Provincial Government, Zhang Yilin, representative of the Jiangsu Fellow Villagers Association, Han Guojun, and Jin Yunpeng, Tang Xiangming, Chen Shufan, Chen Jintao, Xu Jingtang, (Deng Gang) Huang Yanpei, Zhang Yipeng, Master Taixu, and many others.

Gong's Memorial Oration

The memorial oration of the funeral committee members said, "On December 5, 25th year of the Republic of China, Xinzhan, Tiaoyuan, etc., respectfully present clear wine and various delicacies to the spirit of Executive Duan Gong, saying, 'Alas, my lord, the fate of the country is tied to you. When the fate of the country frequently declined, you were the only one who could rectify it. In the late Qing Dynasty, the army was weak and the scholars were depraved. You rose up to revive them, easily changing what was heard and seen. Driving the steeds, whipping the wind and thunder, the fortifications were new, and the sound shook the earth. In Jijiang, you lectured on martial arts, and your intelligence was shared, and all the talents strove to learn, like gold leaping into the forge. You stationed your troops in Yan and Qi, and the soldiers were pleased and the people cherished you. You led the border region, and you were a majestic town in Jianghuai. During the Revolution of 1911, the righteous army rose up, and you pitied the people's hardship and approved the national shame. The consensus was not followed, and the north and south fought against each other. With one declaration, the foundation of the nation was created. You dispelled the chaos and made arrangements properly, expanding the framework and rescuing the people from the fire and water. After deliberating on the change of system, evil thoughts manifested themselves, daring to destroy our room, and still causing obstacles. You fought to the death, opening the door to the dark, relying on justice to maintain the foundation of the country. You held the scales, hoping to express what you had accumulated. The wind and clouds were frightening and chaotic, and Europe was muddy. You made a unique decision, with a broad view and distant hope, supporting justice and attacking violence. The heavenly spear was raised and wielded. When the matter was in full swing, the crowd suspected and slandered you. Finally, you extended the national prestige, running alongside Britain and the United States. The country had many difficulties, and the tyrants indulged themselves. Suddenly, the Han flag was pulled out, and my divine weapon was stolen. You vowed to lead an army, and the Ma Chang campaign was fought at night. The sound of thunder and the comet swept away, and the universe was clear again. For thousands of miles in Mongolia, the tribute was not offered. The control and subjugation were transformed, and the profound plan moved like thunder. These grand plans, the great ones, were clear. Virtue was pleasing to the people, and merit was in the world. You were humble and did not boast, and Taibo yielded three times. The deaf were uniquely discerning, who could spy on your elegant demeanor? The blind and ignorant must ruin their achievements. When you came, the country was righteous, and when you left, the country was falling. Putting the ruler like a game of chess, who will revive the discipline? The second rise was empty and changed, cutting us off. The grand plan was not yet completed, and who cares about the lonely heart? Hao Ran flew far away, following the traces of Ji Ying. When you first took office, the crowd suspected and did not follow you. When you left, they thought together. Late at night, lying in Cangjiang, you were hidden like an enemy country, and the border guards were in turmoil. The sickbed was always sad. Your merits and achievements will shine forever. Your old plans were heroic and strategic, and you used them a hundred times. Only your loyalty, firm, steadfast, and undivided, your great spirit and red heart, sprayed out stars and sun. You should have reached the age of seventy or eighty, protecting the mountains and rivers. You robbed me of an elder statesman. What is the sky saying? The court and the public were shocked and grieved, and hundreds of millions of people wept like rain. The world has lost a teacher, and who will stand with us? Especially we, the confidants, are grateful, and we have been treated with kindness, often close to smiles and words, and we have followed you through hardships, and we have been nurtured in the Jianghu. Once the beam is broken, the cover is feared. The depressions are hidden, and the Huai River is desolate. This man is dead, where can we go? The sea is rising, and there are many fortresses in the four suburbs. The Huabiao has been around for thousands of years, where will the spirit settle? Although the road is separated by clouds, the heroic spirit will not die. I hope that it will descend to the extreme and bless our people. Alas, enjoy it."

Zhao Comes to Meet the Coffin

Chen Juesheng, Director of the Beining Railway Bureau and Chairman of the Hebei-Chahar Transportation Committee, is currently preparing to transport Duan's coffin north on the 7th of this month. Chen is unable to personally meet and greet him due to the busy railway affairs. In addition to ordering the responsible officials of the Beining Railway to take care of the coffin when it is transported from Tianjin to Ping, he also specially sent Zhao Weiru, Director of the Beijing Office of the Railway, to Shanghai to respectfully meet and greet him. Zhao arrived in Shanghai yesterday and stayed at the New Asia Hotel. He immediately went to Duan's residence to pay tribute and discussed the transportation of the coffin with the funeral committee.

Standard for Required Cargo Manifests 102

Ninety Gold Units or More. Customs Announced This Yesterday

The Jianghai Customs, in order to comply with the order to revise the minimum cargo value for cargo manifests not requiring consular certification to ninety gold units, issued Notice No. 1554, stating that: It has been investigated that the minimum cargo value for cargo manifests not requiring consular certification was previously one hundred national currency units, which has now been revised to the equivalent of ninety customs gold units, as announced by this Customs in Notice No. 1499 on February 20th of this year. Now, in accordance with the order of the Ministry of Finance, henceforth, the price of goods requiring cargo manifests shall be based on the standard of exceeding ninety gold units. There is no need to convert it into national currency. If the on-board price of imported goods in each bill of lading is ninety gold units or more, then one consular certified cargo manifest must be issued. If the total price is ninety gold units or less, then there is no need to supplement the manifest. As for the conversion rate between gold units and foreign currencies, it should be calculated in accordance with the government's quarterly regulations and those announced by the Customs. Let all merchants be informed. This is a special notice. Supervisor: Zhu Changnian. Tax Commissioner: Balesen.

Sun Ke and Others Arrive in Shanghai 103

Sun Ke, Wang Zhengting, and Fu Bingchang took the overnight express train from Beijing yesterday and arrived in Shanghai at 7:00 this morning.

Repeated Arbitrary Fines for Invoices. Joint Meeting of Various Industries 104

The Joint Market of Sugar, Seafood, Northern and Southern Goods Industries in this city has recently received reports from members that, in addition to stating the name, quantity, and price of goods sold to various shops in this city on the invoice, and affixing sufficient stamps according to the first category of the stamp tax rate, it is impossible to indicate the total value due to reasons such as tare and deduction. However, the stamp tax inspectors believe it is non-compliant and submit it to the court for trial. The court, without investigating the actual situation, readily imposes a fine of three yuan per invoice. Initially, it was occasional, but recently it has become more frequent. Summons and fines have become exhausting, causing grievances and losses, making it difficult to maintain business. After receiving the report, the market convened a meeting yesterday, attended by more than twenty representatives from the sugar, seafood, southern goods, northern goods, cooked food, longan, exchange, and pickled mustard tuber industries. Qiu Yangzhi presided over the meeting, and Xue Meiting recorded the proceedings. It was believed that the suffering experienced by various industries in the city must be widespread. If they do not appeal for correction, how can they alleviate the hardship? It was decided to state the facts, cite the Ministry of Finance's Decree No. 11462, and jointly send a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for assistance, convene an expanded meeting of all relevant industries in the city as soon as possible, and jointly request the government to quickly rectify the situation to avoid harassment and ensure business stability.

Jiang Fangzhen Speaks Freely on Observations Regarding the German-Japanese-Italian Agreement 106

Mr. Jiang Fangzhen, a well-known figure in the army, spoke to a reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency yesterday about his observations on the German-Japanese agreement and the Italian-Japanese exchange of recognition of Italy's annexation of Abyssinia and the puppet state of Manchukuo. Mr. Jiang, having recently visited Italy, Germany, and Japan, offered unique insights. The following is a record of his remarks:

Italy Does Not Wish to Conflict with Russia

Mr. Jiang first stated that Italy's eastward policy is aimed at the Near East, not the Far East. The Near East—Turkey, Romania, Yugoslavia, and Afghanistan—has formed an alliance. Czechoslovakia is allied with France, and France is allied with Soviet Russia, and they all communicate with Soviet Russia. Mussolini is extremely intelligent and understands this situation. For the sake of his eastward policy, he knows that he cannot offend Soviet Russia. Now, the German-Japanese agreement uses anti-communism to resist Soviet Russia. Italy is not foolish and will definitely not participate.

Recognition of the Puppet State of Manchukuo is Also Unlikely

Based on the above, Italy's policy is in the Near East, not the Far East, so it does not want to interfere in the affairs between China and Japan. As for the current agreement between Italy and Japan, I am afraid that Italy will not formally recognize the puppet state of Manchukuo. As far as I know, Italy's establishment of a consulate in Shenyang is temporary, with a term of one year. Italy is currently trying to woo Britain. If Italy considers the things that Britain is unwilling to do in the Far East, it will also be unwilling to do them itself. Moreover, Italy is trying to expand its market in China. Why would it hurt China's feelings because of this? Moreover, the relationship between Italy and Japan has not been very good in the past. Japan had coveted Abyssinia and once planned to send the daughter of a count to marry the prince of Awa, but Italy was jealous and stopped it, preventing the good deed from happening.

Japan's Gains Do Not Outweigh Its Losses

Speaking of Japan's recognition of Italy's annexation of Abyssinia, it is nothing more than to restore trade with Abyssinia. Since the European War, Japan has exported tens of millions of goods to Abyssinia every year. Now that Abyssinia is occupied by Italy, Japan is naturally unwilling to give up its market in Abyssinia. Therefore, it has no choice but to recognize Italy's annexation of Abyssinia in order to seek Italy's recognition of its rights and interests in Abyssinia. In this regard, Italy has indeed made considerable concessions and approved it. However, we believe that Japan's valuation is not worth the loss. Japan has always regarded itself as the elder brother of the colored people. Now, recognizing Italy's annexation of Abyssinia is tantamount to slapping itself in the face. Japan previously wanted to develop its power in India and repeatedly approached Gandhi and Tagore in the movement, but all were rejected. In recent years, it has also approached the Philippines. The result of recognizing Italy's annexation of Abyssinia will make it even more despised by the colored people of the East and cut off its own path.

Japanese Public Opinion at Home is Dissatisfied

After the German-Japanese agreement was established, the Japanese officialdom was initially complacent, thinking it was a diplomatic victory, but public opinion did not think so. When I returned to China this time, I passed through Japan and saw that its domestic newspapers were very indifferent to this and did not have a good opinion. Japan once said that it did not want to interfere in European affairs. Isn't it throwing itself into the European vortex by allying with Germany and Italy? This is what its people oppose. When I was in Germany, I heard Germans say that Germany's alliance with Japan was just perfunctory. Moreover, Japan's active approach to China is purely at the suggestion of the military. The financial groups and the people are dissatisfied. One thing proves this: since Matsuoka took over as the president of the South Manchurian Railway Company, the price of each share has fallen by two yuan. Previously, the capitalists planned to invest, but the military stopped them. Now, the military is calling for investment, but the capitalists are unwilling. For example, the recent advocacy of investment in North China is mostly hesitant. The capitalists are afraid that if the military changes its mind one day, all previous efforts will inevitably be in vain.

Chamber of Commerce Sends a Petition to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for the Prompt Conclusion of a Reciprocal Treaty with South Africa 107

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce sent a petition to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs yesterday, stating: "To the Nanjing Ministry of Foreign Affairs: We have recently received a letter from Cen Xinyi and Liang Juekuang, representatives of overseas Chinese returning from South Africa, regarding the implementation of harsh regulations and the mistreatment of overseas Chinese in South Africa. They have sent representatives back to China to request the government to negotiate and conclude a reciprocal trade treaty, or to continue the previous Sino-South African gentlemen's agreement. The original text, in addition to being submitted directly by the representatives, is omitted here. The letter concludes: 'We dare to report to your council, requesting your assistance to save our compatriots.' Based on this, although there are only a few thousand overseas Chinese in South Africa, it is a suitable market for the sale of Chinese goods and is currently in a period of development. It is imperative to actively proceed with negotiating a reciprocal treaty. Yesterday, we read in the newspaper that your ministry has appointed Zhang Shoumo as the new consul-general in South Africa. It would be best to authorize Consul-General Zhang to pay attention to handling this matter in order to achieve the goal of reciprocity. In addition to the petition from the representatives, we hereby telegraph this to your ministry for review. We earnestly request that you consider the difficulties of our compatriots and provide prompt assistance."

Lan Enbao Passed Away Yesterday 108

Colonel Lan Enbao, an American advisor and commander at the Hangzhou Central Aviation Academy, suddenly died of heart failure at his residence at 7:00 yesterday morning. His remains were transported to Shanghai by hearse in the afternoon. Mr. Lan was known to be in good health, so the news of his death came as a shock to many. According to reports, Mr. Lan had only arrived in China from the United States two months ago. When he passed through Shanghai, it was only for a few days. His wife also resided in Hangzhou.

Commodity Inspection Bureau Inspects Raw Silk Quality 110

Excellent Results Build Confidence at Home and Abroad; Plans to Add More Manpower and Equipment

The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau's inspection of raw silk originally only enforced compulsory inspection of the weight. The quality inspection was left to the free decision of the silk merchants. This year, the Ministry of Industry, believing that the overseas silk market requires a large quantity of uniform-quality goods, which cannot compete with other countries without implementing compulsory raw silk quality inspection, ordered the bureau to implement raw silk quality inspection from August 1st. Since its implementation, it has gained the trust of Chinese and foreign silk merchants. It is reported that foreign silk industry organizations have repeatedly decided to write to the bureau to praise the accuracy of the inspection. Silk trade based on the bureau's inspection certificate is promising. However, the bureau's current manpower and equipment for raw silk inspection can only inspect about 300 bales of raw silk per day, while the daily reported quantity often reaches more than 400 bales. The responsible personnel of the bureau's silk group supervise the staff to intensify their work, working day and night, but it is still difficult to cope. The bureau is now planning to report to the Ministry of Industry to add to the budget and appropriately expand the manpower and equipment in order to cope with the current situation, so that the general silk merchants can be more satisfied and to prepare for the compulsory implementation of raw silk grade inspection in February next year.

Lianyi Society's Dispute with Employees; Two Fellow-Provincial Associations Mediate 112

The No. 4 District Civil Boat Carriers' Union and the Guangbang Lianyi Society had a dispute over the issue of employees, which had been unresolved for a long time. Yesterday afternoon, the Ningbo and Guangdong fellow-provincial associations specially consulted to mediate. The Ningbo fellow-provincial association was represented by Mao Heyuan, Zhang Jiguang, Chu Qiaqing, Jin Tingsun, Wu Yaqin, and Tang Xinqin; the Guangdong fellow-provincial association was represented by Li Dachao, Guo Qiming, Guo Zhongliang, and Chen Qifen. Yu Qiaqing presided over the meeting. After reviewing the written opinions of both parties, the following three measures were proposed: (1) All fruit cases of the commercial firms belonging to the Lianyi Hall shall continue to be handled by the workers of the Civil Boat Carriers' Union, and one cent (i.e., one copper coin) shall be added to the original price per case. (2) The issue of new workers leaving or staying shall be properly handled by the trade union. (3) In the future, workers should fulfill their duties and not be lazy, which shall be the responsibility of the trade union. Based on the above three principles, Guo Qiming of the Guangdong fellow-provincial association was appointed to draft an agreement, which would then be reviewed. However, the investor side stated to the fellow-provincial association that the investor has the right to independently hire workers. The two associations decided to postpone the mediation.

Qiu Jiyu Confesses to Participating in the Murder of Tang Youren; Court Reschedules Trial for the 16th to Be Heard Jointly with Liu Zhennan's Case 113

Tang Youren, the former Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, Minister of Transportation, and advisor to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, from Hunan, was assassinated in front of his private residence at No. 12 Gan Cun, Ganxi Road, French Concession, at around 5:00 p.m. on December 25th of last year. The murderer fled the scene immediately. After the French Police Department and our government offered a reward for his arrest, the Public Concession Police Department cracked a theft case in June or July of this year and arrested six bandits, including Qiu Jiyu, and seized a handgun. It was found that this gun was the same as the one used to kill Tang. After the Special No. 1 Court sentenced the theft case, the French Police Department took Qiu and others back and sent them to the Special No. 2 Court for interrogation and investigation. Because Qiu and others denied participating in the Tang case and there was no conclusive evidence, they were not prosecuted. Qiu and the other six defendants were sent back to the Special No. 1 Court for execution. Recently, the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau arrested Liu Zhennan, a suspect in the Tang case, who confessed that Qiu Jiyu and several others, including those surnamed Yang, Xiao, and Xiang, were involved. Liu was transferred to the Special No. 2 Court and sent to the Police Department for investigation. On the 30th of last month, Judge Wang of the Special No. 2 Court held a hearing and prohibited spectators. As a result, the court ordered further investigation and rescheduled the hearing for the 16th of this month. At the same time, the French Police Department requested the Special No. 2 Court to prepare a document to send detectives to transfer Qiu Jiyu to court for interrogation. The details of the case have been reported in this newspaper. It is now known that Qiu was transferred from the Special No. 1 Court on the previous day by detectives Dai Rongji and Zuo Qihong of the French Police Department with a document. It was found that Qiu Jiyu, also known as Zhao Xiangbao and Zhao Qiyu, was 26 years old and originally from Shengxian County, Zhejiang. He had previously committed a kidnapping case and was sentenced to five years by the French Concession Court. After serving his sentence, he was sent to the inland government for interrogation. After serving his sentence, the Special No. 2 Court reviewed the case and sentenced him to five years and two months of imprisonment. The number of days in prison was counted as execution. Qiu committed the crime of participating in the assassination of Tang Youren after being released after serving his sentence for the kidnapping case. He escaped and was later arrested and imprisoned for theft. When questioned about the Tang case, he confessed without hesitation. At noon yesterday, he was escorted to the Special No. 2 Court, where Judge Sun Pengxian, accompanied by clerk Tao Zongkan, held a hearing in the Criminal Division. Gu Shouxi, a lawyer from the Police Department, stated the facts of the case and requested that the hearing be rescheduled to the 16th to be heard jointly with Liu Zhennan's case, and that spectators be prohibited due to the importance of the case. The court approved the request and rescheduled the hearing for the 16th to be heard jointly with Liu Zhennan's case. It is reported that Qiu confessed to participating in the assassination and that he was the one who fired the gun.

Chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Council, Arnold, Speaks on Finances 114

Says That in Order to Balance Income and Expenditure, It Is Necessary to Increase the Patrol Tax

Mr. Arnold, Chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Council, spoke at a meeting of the British Association on Friday on the financial situation of the Municipal Council, stating that since 1929, the ordinary income of the Municipal Council has been insufficient to cover expenditure every year. Since 1932, funds have been allocated from the gold stored in the electricity facilities to make up for the shortfall. This gold is now almost exhausted, so it is necessary to find other ways to balance the budget. In the past three years, major efforts have been made to economize, saving 3.5 million yuan. Major expenditures that are absolutely necessary have been postponed. The only stable policy being pursued is to balance income and expenditure, and it is inevitable to increase the patrol tax and borrow money to cover major expenditures. If we continue not to balance the budget, it will gradually become difficult to borrow money on reasonable terms to cover major expenditures. Due to the recent austerity measures, savings have been made in the fire brigade, public works, the office of the general manager of the business community, the intelligence office, and the rickshaw office, totaling 70,000 yuan. Together with the results of the Staff Committee's proposals, 106,000 yuan can be saved, totaling 176,000 yuan. However, most of this will only be implemented in 1937, and full implementation will require until 1938. Therefore, the shortfall for this year, calculated based on the figures for the first half of the year, amounts to 3.25 million yuan. The original budget estimated the shortfall at 2 million yuan, which was to be made up by allocating funds from the reserve fund, but this fund is almost exhausted as a result. However, the actual shortfall exceeds the estimate by more than 60%, so major economies must be made next year in order to overcome the difficulties. We will start the year with a shortfall of 1.25 million yuan, so the 1937 budget, excluding the aforementioned savings, will amount to 4 million yuan, accounting for 4% of the patrol tax. It is not known how the shortfall for this year and next year will be made up. The measure of greatly increasing the patrol tax will be unavoidable. If it can be increased by 2% and borrow money to make up for the remaining estimated shortfall and to cover the required major expenditures, then by 1938, when the aforementioned savings can be fully realized, the debts on the books can be cleared at once. Thus, an increase of 2% in the patrol tax will be sufficient to meet future needs. If we delay longer, the amount of the increase in the patrol tax will be higher. If we do not adopt a stable policy as soon as possible and allow the shortfall to extend for another year or two, I am afraid that the patrol tax will inevitably increase by 4%. If it is increased by 2%, those who pay 100 yuan in rent per month will only have to pay 25 yuan in tax per year, or those who pay 200 yuan in rent per month will only have to pay 48 yuan in tax. Mr. Arnold finally spoke of the reasons for hastily adopting the report of the Economic Committee without first giving the staff the opportunity to comment, saying that it was because the budget for next year was being drafted and the committee's proposals had to be implemented as soon as possible.
