Tobacco Advisor Niu Sen Assassinated - Tax Administration Sends Telegram to Investigate - Xuchang Tobacco Company Not Government-Run 122

According to the Kuomintang News Agency, reports state that Niu Sen, an American advisor to the Nanjing government and manager of the government-run Xuchang Tobacco Company, was shot and killed in Xuchang, and the motive of the perpetrators was largely resentment towards the official operation of the tobacco business. The reporter specifically went to the Taxation Department of the Ministry of Finance to investigate the truth of the matter. According to the person in charge of the department, the department had previously ordered a large number of tobacco seeds from the United States and transported them to Xuchang and other places to distribute to farmers because the tobacco leaves produced in various parts of our country were produced using traditional methods, and farmers did not know how to improve cultivation, resulting in a decline in product quality and sales. The department also hired American tobacco experts to guide planting to improve the quality of tobacco and cultivate tax sources. Niu Sen, an American citizen, was the department's hired expert advisor for the improvement of tobacco leaves. He has been in office for four years and has made great contributions to improving tobacco leaves and providing guidance. The department has reported that Niu Sen was assassinated in Xuchang. According to the report of the American Tobacco Improvement Committee, the department has telegraphed the Yuzhong Tax Administration Office to investigate the cause and has discussed with the local authorities to strictly arrest the perpetrators. The Xuchang Tobacco Company is purely a commercial company and not government-run. The department's American Tobacco Improvement Committee is a technical organization dedicated to improving tobacco leaves. The reports in various newspapers that the government operates the tobacco business are not true.

Wages Robbed from Shenxin No. 9 Factory - Iron Box Snatcher Shot - Guard Wu Zishan Pursues Robbers - Robber Wang Shaohua Shot in Six Places - Original Stolen 1800 Yuan Recovered 123

The Shenxin No. 9 Cotton Mill in Macao Road, western Shanghai, has a large number of male and female workers, so its wages are paid daily. At 9:05 PM the night before last, Gu Zuyu, the accountant of Shenxin No. 9 Factory, from Wuxi, and foreman Zhu Guojun were preparing to issue wages when two robbers suddenly broke in, each holding a pistol, forbidding anyone from making a sound. They snatched a small iron box containing 1800 yuan in legal tender from the accountant's table and fled. When they ran out the door, they were spotted by Wu Zishan, a Hua detective No. 767 guarding the factory gate. Seeing one of the robbers fleeing with an iron box, he knew they were robbers and blew his whistle and drew his self-defense pistol, chasing after them and firing three shots. One of the robbers fell in response, while the other escaped. The injured robber was apprehended, a "lotus sprinkler" pistol with five bullets was seized, and the stolen 1800 yuan was recovered. The incident was reported to the Putuo Road Police Station, which sent detectives to transport the injured robber to the police hospital. The injured robber was identified as Wang Shaohua, 35 years old, from Nanjing, with six gunshot wounds to his abdomen, waist, and right leg (as the bullets had all passed through). He was kept in the hospital for treatment. Yesterday morning, Zhang Tianyin, a lawyer from the police station, reported the incident to Judge Huang Risheng of the Eighth Criminal Division of the First Special Court, requesting a postponement. He stated that at around 6:00 AM this morning, the police had also found a "lotus sprinkler" pistol with five bullets inside the Shenxin No. 9 Factory, which was thought to have been dropped by one of the escaping robbers. However, it is suspected that the robbery of Shenxin No. 9 Factory was the result of collaboration with insiders, as the back door of the factory, located on Moganshan Road, was originally equipped with a very large secret lock, which was found to have been replaced after the incident. Subsequently, Gu Zuyu, the accountant, testified to the robbery, and Judge Huang postponed the case, awaiting Wang Shaohua's recovery before further questioning.

Capital Express - Maintaining Punctuality - Various Discount and Free Tickets Not Applicable - Station Staff and Passengers Should Prepare in Advance 124

The Ministry of Railways believes that the "Capital Express" on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway is about to operate. However, because the number of seats on the train is limited, various discount or free tickets are not applicable, and official cars cannot be added. With the approval of the Executive Yuan, it will be handled in accordance with the precedent before the opening of the Shanghai-Ping express. The relevant order from the ministry states: "It is hereby ordered that it shall be dealt with in accordance with the Executive Yuan's Instruction No. 6288 dated October 24, 1936, and the National Government's Instruction No. 788 dated October 21, 1936. Regarding the opening of a high-speed special express train between Nanjing and Shanghai on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, named the 'Capital Express', it is proposed to follow the precedent of the Shanghai-Ping express. In addition to round-trip tickets, all kinds of official travel passes, all kinds of discount and free tickets, and preferential tickets will not be applicable to the 'Capital Express'. Furthermore, due to the shorter travel time and the limited number of cars, this train shall not be used for private cars to maintain income and show restrictions. Please notify and order compliance, as requested in the memorandum submitted by the Secretariat of this Committee to the Executive Yuan, which stated that the Executive Yuan had approved the Ministry of Railways' memorandum, in order to open a high-speed special express train between Nanjing and Shanghai on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, named the 'Capital Express'. It is proposed to follow the precedent of the Shanghai-Ping express. In addition to round-trip tickets, all kinds of official travel passes, all kinds of discount and free tickets, and preferential tickets will not be applicable to the 'Capital Express'. Furthermore, due to the shorter travel time and the limited number of cars, this train shall not be used for private cars to maintain income and show restrictions. Please notify and order compliance, etc., which was approved at the 81st meeting of this Yuan and sent to the Central Political Committee, instructing them to verify and forward the matter. After deliberation, it was reported to the 24th meeting of this Committee and approved. In addition to notifying the Central Executive Committee, the case shall be filed, and a copy of the original letter shall be sent for verification and notification, and an order shall be given to comply, etc. This should be dealt with in accordance with the above. In addition to replying by letter and distributing the order, the attached document shall be copied and ordered to be followed, and those under its jurisdiction shall be ordered to comply, etc., by order, etc., this shall be complied with, etc., this is the order," etc. It is heard that as the express train has been sped up, it is essential not to miss the travel time. The Traffic Department of the road has separately ordered the following measures to maintain punctuality: (1) Before the train arrives at the station, the stationmaster on duty should instruct the relevant staff to be stationed at the service location, plan and arrange all necessary matters in advance, and place outbound luggage and packages in suitable locations. The stacking of luggage and packages must have a specific sequence and location to avoid difficulties at the loading and unloading stations. Other procedures for handling receipt, delivery, and signing must also be as fast and simple as possible. (2) If there is a large amount or heavy luggage and packages to be shipped out, sufficient porters should be prepared in advance to quickly load and transport them, ensuring that it is completed within the specified time. At the same time, the loading and unloading stations must be notified so that they can be prepared. Once the departure time is reached, loading and unloading should be stopped. Any luggage and packages left behind should be kept and transported on the next earliest train. (3) Outbound travelers should be informed by the stationmaster on duty, the station police, and the station staff of the appropriate location to stand in order to board the train calmly and avoid rushing around. If passengers are carrying heavy or large quantities of hand luggage, they should be advised to put it in the luggage compartment. The elderly, the young, and passengers with slow movement should be assisted by station staff to board the train. If the departure time has arrived, the train should be ordered to depart immediately. If there are still passengers who have not boarded the train after the train has started, they should be advised to take the next earliest train and not stop the train again. (4) Before the train arrives at the stopping station, the train staff should notify the passengers getting off the train to prepare in advance to avoid being rushed and delaying the travel time. (5) Other trains related to the "Capital Express" should also strictly maintain their punctuality to avoid interfering with the meeting and causing delays. (6) If special circumstances are discovered, other related stations should be notified immediately to prepare in advance to avoid delaying the travel time.

A Scoundrel in the Medical Profession Actually Solicits Patients for Profit - Xu Jisheng in Front of Renji Hospital - Doctor Cuts Off Name and Address on Prescriptions 130

The number of stomach doctors in this city is increasing daily, but regardless of whether the doctors are genuine or not, they all compete for business, except for a few famous doctors. The methods of competition were originally limited to publicity, but recently there has been a method of soliciting patients. In front of major hospitals, those who seek treatment are temporarily solicited, which not only affects the reputation of Chinese and Western doctors but also greatly harms the health of the population. Renji Hospital had previously detained Xu Jisheng, who was lingering in front of the hospital to solicit patients, and sent him to the police station. He was lightly reprimanded and released because he had not committed any illegal acts. Xu was soliciting business for Liu Baoguang (also known as Liu Songshi), a Cantonese who runs the Baoguang Hospital at No. 47 South Tiantong Road, Hongkou. Therefore, after being reprimanded and released, he still relied on Liu for a living. At 11:30 AM on the 4th, Gu Boyu, a woman living north of Hanqiao, brought her daughter Gu Yunzhen to Renji Hospital for throat treatment. Just as they arrived at the hospital gate and asked about the throat department, a person approached Gu and said that the throat doctor in the hospital would not be in until the afternoon. If they needed treatment, he could take them to his house to avoid delay. He then hired a rickshaw for Gu and her daughter and led the car to the intersection of South Tiantong Road. Xu Jisheng, who was originally lingering there, saw them and, knowing that they were seeking medical treatment, invited Gu and her daughter into the hospital. Gu paid the registration fee of one yuan and the registration fee of two cents. Afterwards, Gu asked the people in the hospital when the doctor would go to Renji. At that time, Liu Songshi was sitting in the consulting room. Hearing this, he immediately claimed to be a doctor and said that he only went to Renji every afternoon, and he also had to treat patients at Baolong and Guangci Hospitals. After examining Gu's daughter and writing a prescription, he suddenly cut off the part of the prescription that had the doctor's name and address printed on it. Gu thought that the important part of the prescription was the doctor's name and address. If the prescription did not have this mark, it would be as if the doctor was not responsible, so she argued with Liu. Liu knew that Gu was not easy to deceive and replaced it with a full prescription. However, after Gu took her daughter home, she felt that Liu's actions were suspicious, so she did not get the medicine and instead took her daughter to Renji Hospital to inquire if there was a doctor named Liu among the hospital's throat doctors. The hospital found out that there was no doctor Liu. Gu laughed it off. Unexpectedly, when she left the hospital, she saw Xu Jisheng recruiting patients for Liu there again. She immediately informed the hospital authorities, who reported it to the police station, and detectives were sent to arrest Xu. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the First Special District Local Court. Judge Ye interrogated him, and police lawyer Qian Xunjiu explained the incident and requested that Xu be detained for further investigation. Gu also came to court to testify to everything. In light of Xu's testimony that he was soliciting business for Liu Songshi and did not receive fixed remuneration, the court ordered Xu Jisheng to be detained for further hearing on the 8th of this month.

Yang Yushan and Others Engage in Anomalous Behavior by Impersonating Officials and Swindling Money; Dismissed County Magistrate Solicits Lawsuits in Front of the Courthouse; Longhua Monk Refuses Payment for Failed Efforts; Judge Opens Trial, Defendants Deny Involvement 131

Yang Yushan from Yixing, 42 years old, residing at No. 6 in front of the Shanghai Local Court, ran the Yang Fuxing Coal and Charcoal Shop. Wang Bingquan from Hunan, also known as Wang Bingjun and Wang Yaozu, 49 years old, a graduate of Anhui Political Science School, passed the county magistrate examination and was assigned to Zhejiang. Due to a case, he was dismissed from his position, his wife and children left him, and he was destitute. He set up a character splitting stall in front of the Shanghai Local Court. After July of this year, he became a permanent clerk in the Local Court. Sun Yuchen from Hangzhou, 33 years old, residing in Tiande Lane, Haichao Road, was a freight company broker. These three were usually very close. Yang Yushan, at No. 1 Renlin Lane, Huanghe Road (i.e., Rue Laguerre) in the French Concession, co-founded the Zhengchi Law Firm to make a living, specializing in soliciting lawsuits. Wang Bingquan and Sun Yuchen also frequently visited. In May of this year, a case occurred at Shanghai Longhua Temple where Deputy Abbot Hong Kui committed sodomy on a temple worker, Yang Shouchang, and was sued for theft and detention. Hong Kui's disciple, Abbot Daheng, hired lawyer Yang Maoqian to handle the case. At the same time, Hong Kui's friend, Gan Tianran, went with Abbot Daheng to the Zhengchi Law Firm to ask Yang Yushan to find a way in court. Yang Yushan impersonated a court clerk, claiming to know the judge handling the case and demanded 500 yuan, guaranteeing bail and acquittal. Abbot Daheng later learned that Hong Kui was sentenced to three years and two months, and the bail never materialized. The promised money was not paid. The incident came to light when the court received a letter addressed to Yang Yushan, Court Clerk, from someone named Kuifa, revealing the fraudulent situation in the Hong Kui case. The Local Court found that there was no Yang Yushan among the court clerks and ordered the deceased Chief Clerk Xuan Maohe to investigate the previous situation and arrest Yang Yushan, transferring him to the Prosecutor's Office for investigation by Prosecutor Mei Yinjie. The Second Special District Court was requested to assist in the search of the Zhengchi Law Firm organized by Yang. At the same time, a letter from Sun Yuchen to Wang Bingquan was found, stating, "At 11 o'clock, I received a call from Liu Lin (i.e., Lin Sheng), mentioning that the money has not been collected yet and needs to be discussed again in the afternoon... (omitted)... The complaint from Du Akang has been signed. If Liu Linsheng comes again, please sign that one hundred yuan cannot settle the matter (omitted)..." The letter ended with "Just say the summons has been issued, and it may not be resolved immediately." Judging from the wording, there was clear evidence of joint fraud. Wang Bingquan and Sun Yuchen were subsequently arrested and detained, and all visitation was suspended. Multiple investigative hearings were held. Yang denied all accusations, but Chief Clerk Xuan's investigation report proved that Yang did indeed claim to be a court clerk, claiming to know nine out of ten judges and even said after the verdict that he could ask Judge Wu Xiangzu to correct it, but his one hundred yuan was not paid and would only be paid when his master was released. Based on the seized letter, the Liu Linsheng case was investigated and found to be where Du Akang accused his wife, Ding Aying, of adultery with Liu Linsheng. The three jointly defrauded Liu Linsheng of 100 yuan, which was also confirmed during testimony and the money was never paid. It was also heard that Yang Yushan, Wang Bingquan, and Sun Yuchen were attacking each other in court, allegedly due to uneven distribution of the fraudulent proceeds. Wang Bingquan, acting as a clerk, first sent the letter signed Kuifa to Yang Yushan, intentionally sending it to the Local Court, as the new President Lu and Chief Clerk Yi had just taken office and were determined to take swift action. Yang was thus caught in the net. After Yang was arrested, he implicated Wang Bingquan and Sun Yuchen in court, but the search resulted in the discovery of evidence of fraud, leading to their collective downfall, a true result of mutual destruction. Therefore, the prosecutor, based on the investigation results, charged Yang Yushan with impersonating a public official and defrauding money, but since the money was not obtained, he should be charged with attempted fraud. Wang Bingquan and Sun Yuchen were also charged with attempted fraud. Yesterday, Judge Zhang Peiming opened the trial. The defendants all denied the allegations, and their attitudes were not as combative as during the investigative hearings, as they each attempted to exonerate themselves. The judge, because the witnesses in this case were not all present, ordered the case to be adjourned for further hearing.

Dong Xianguang Resigns as Manager of Three Agencies, Cui Weiwu Succeeds Him 133

The three agencies, *Shishi Xinbao*, *Da Wanbao*, and *Shenshi Electric News Agency*, have been reorganizing since April of last year when General Manager Zhang Zhuping resigned. Initially, Du Yuesheng acted as the general manager, followed by Wei Daoming, who was appointed by the board of directors. Later, due to Wei's departure abroad, Dong Xianguang was invited to act as an agent by a joint meeting of the three agencies' directors and supervisors. Now, Dong has expressed his resignation to the board of directors, citing his numerous concurrent positions making it difficult to manage the affairs of the three agencies effectively. Yesterday afternoon at 4 PM, the three agencies' directors and supervisors held a joint meeting at the New Asia Building on North Sichuan Road. The directors and supervisors present acknowledged Dong's active reorganization of the three agencies internally since his appointment, which had achieved remarkable results. They repeatedly and sincerely urged him to stay, but Dong's intention to resign was firm. Consequently, Director Cui Weiwu was recommended to succeed Dong as the general manager of the three agencies. Cui has many years of experience in the news industry and is highly knowledgeable. His acceptance of this challenging role is expected to be a pleasant success. The colleagues of the three agencies have expressed their support, it is said.

1. China Bookstore, Shareholders Meeting Yesterday

2.

China Bookstore Co., Ltd. originally scheduled its 26th annual shareholders' meeting for yesterday afternoon at the Ningbo Native Place Association in Shanghai. However, based on a temporary proposal from shareholders, it was changed to a temporary meeting. It was decided to change the accounting year to run from January 1st to the end of December as one year. The 25th accounting period, which was originally set to end at the end of June of the 25th year, was changed to end at the end of December of the 25th year. It was also resolved to increase the capital by two million yuan, bringing the total capital to four million yuan. Old shareholders will subscribe to four shares for every five shares they hold, leaving 20% for employees, staff, and those connected to the cultural field. All of these were passed, but because the number of households present did not exceed half, the resolution was considered provisional. It was decided to convene a second shareholders' meeting on the 27th of this month in accordance with Article 186 of the Company Law, it is said.

1. Han Changlin Denies Participating in Murder, Related to Tang Jikun's "Rhapsody" Case

2.

Tang Jikun, also known as Xiao Qiao, a Chaozhou native, who resided at No. 29 Bao'an Fang, Dongxin Bridge Street, French Concession, made a substantial profit selling red pills. This attracted the covetousness and blackmail attempts of ruffians and hooligans. On July 20th of the 22nd year, at 8:00 AM, Tang was walking outside, passing the entrance of Baoxing Li, Dongxin Bridge Street, when he was dragged by five or six hooligans in front of No. 14 Baoxing Li. When their blackmail attempt failed, the hooligans lifted Tang's limbs and violently threw him to the ground in a move commonly called "arranging three and earth", causing Tang's death from injuries. Afterwards, the French police arrested a suspect named A Si Mapizi, who was handed over to the Second Special Court for prosecution and sentenced to five years in prison. He has now served his term and been released. At that time, according to the suspect's confession, he and other fugitives, including Xue A'gen (aka Xiao Suzhou), Zhao A'er, Zhang Zhulin, Xiao Long, a countryman, and Xiao Changlin (aka Han Changlin), jointly blackmailed Tang. When that failed, they killed him. The French police immediately dispatched detectives to arrest the fugitives. In January of the 24th year, Xue A'gen, the principal offender in the case, was apprehended and sent to the Special Court, where he was sentenced to twelve years in prison after interrogation. The offender appealed to the Third Higher Branch Court, which reduced the sentence to eight years. The offender still dissatisfied, appealed to the Supreme Court, which has now ordered a retrial. The circumstances of the initial investigation by the Third Higher Branch Court have been reported in this newspaper. Now, Yang Yilong, an investigator for the French police, discovered that Han Changlin, aka Xiao Changlin, age 23, a native of Pudong and an accomplice in the case, was hiding at No. 112 Huadong Li, Kunming Road, Hongkou. He and the Public Concession Police apprehended Han at noon the day before yesterday. Yesterday, he was handed over to the Second Special Court. Judge Sun Pengwei interrogated him in the First Criminal Tribunal. Gu Shouxi, a lawyer from the Police Department, stated the case and requested an extension for further investigation before proceeding with the trial. During the interrogation, Han confessed to knowing that Xiao Suzhou, Xue A'gen, and others had killed Tang, but he had not participated. He said that someone had reported him out of spite because he had refused to lend them money, resulting in his arrest. The court adjourned the hearing to the 15th and ordered the defendant to be detained.

1. Slick Bookstore Commits Fraud, Sui Zhuru Accused of Swindling and Corrupting Morals, Book Industry Association Investigation Confirms

2.

Sui Zhuru, a 32-year-old native of Dantu, opened the "Slick Cultural Bookstore" at No. 32 Gufuli, Baoshan Road, Zhabei. He mailed out a large number of book catalogs, making exaggerated claims and extensively advertising with announcements such as "Grand Opening," "Huge Sale," and "Free Gifts." In reality, there wasn't a single book in the catalog, and the so-called "Grand Building" was a dilapidated house sublet from someone else. The so-called "Various Paintings and Calligraphy" were nude photographs and pornographic books like "The Tinder Monk" and "Garbage Cart." Wang Shounan, from the Yuanchangfu Medicine and Candy Shop in Jingxian, Anhui, saw the exaggerated advertisement and remitted one yuan and thirty-nine cents in national currency to the store on March 21st of this year to purchase the books listed in the catalog, but they were never sent. He then sent a letter to the Shanghai Book Industry Association, requesting an investigation. The association sent a representative, Yuan Xifan, along with the relevant police department to search the premises. They uncovered various pornographic books and pictures. Sui was arrested and sent to the local court, where Prosecutor Lei charged him with fraud under Articles 235 and 123 of the Criminal Code, as well as corrupting morals. Yesterday, Judge Xie Zhengji opened the court session. Sui confessed that the "Grand Building" announcement was for promotional purposes and that the books in the catalog did exist. He also claimed that the books Wang Shounan had purchased had been sent, and that the pornographic pictures and books had been obtained from elsewhere. He retained lawyer Dan Yu to defend him. At this point, Yuan Xifan went to court to provide detailed evidence of Sui's "Slick Bookstore" practices. The judge immediately declared the debate closed and scheduled the verdict for the 10th of this month.

1. Attention Pilgrims Wishing to Go to the Philippines, Registration Closes on the 15th of this Month, Departure from Shanghai on January 26th

2.

The Catholic International Eucharistic Congress is scheduled to be held in Manila, the capital of the Philippines, from February 3rd to 7th, 1937. The Pope has specially appointed an envoy to Manila to preside over the ceremony. Cardinals, priests, and male and female Catholics from Europe and the United States will travel to the Philippines for the pilgrimage and the ceremony. Many have pre-chartered special vessels. The situation is extremely enthusiastic. The meaning of the Congress is to respectfully welcome the Holy Body of Jesus, to parade and pray for world peace, and to bless the people. Since its establishment over sixty years ago, it has been held every two years in cities around the world. Each Congress has been attended by hundreds of thousands of believers. This is the first time it is being held in Asia, making it a truly rare and grand event. The Papal Representative to China, Archbishop Cai, has appointed Lu Bohong, President of the Catholic Action Association of China, to organize a pilgrimage group. The group is scheduled to depart on January 26th next year on the North German Company's "Bosten" cruise ship. It will return from Manila in 10 days and arrive in Shanghai in 14 days. The round-trip fare is 250 yuan for first class and 210 yuan for second class. The cost of food and lodging in Manila for 10 days is approximately 100 yuan per person. The congress is approaching quickly. Catholics in the country who wish to go should quickly report to Mr. Geng at the Catholic Action Association at Dongjiadu in the South City in order to reserve cabins and apply for passports to leave the country. Registration will close on December 15th, it is said.

1. Dispute Over Embezzlement by Employees of North China Coal Company, Plaintiff Files Civil Suit, Defendant Claims Forced to Write False Accounts

2.

Hu Jingqing, the manager of the North China Coal Company branch on the corner of Meierxi Ai Road and Ladu Road (residing at No. 35, Lane 286, Ladu Road), recently reported to the French police that Qiu Wenhao (a native of Ningbo), an employee, had embezzled 1,392.25 yuan from December of last year to September of this year, taking advantage of his position managing coal. It was discovered that he had spent 76 yuan at the sales department and had deposited 200 yuan into the Shanghai Citizen Bank. He had also deposited 313.93 yuan into the Bank of China under the alias Qiu. The person then went into hiding. Later, his brother, Qiu Jinzhang, sent a receipt book from his hometown, which was considered evidence of concealing evidence. Hu requested an investigation. The police chief approved the request, filed the case, and handed it over to the Second Special Court for public prosecution. The plaintiff also hired a lawyer to file a civil suit. Yesterday, Judge Sun Pengwei conducted a trial in the First Criminal Tribunal. The plaintiff presented a paper embezzled account written by the defendant. The defendant was interrogated and denied any embezzlement. Regarding the deposits, he said that they were the result of years of hard work. The account presented by the plaintiff was forced to be written, When I wrote this account, the plaintiff explained to me that after writing it, I could still continue to do business, so I wrote it. But the above has forced to write false account four words, Now the plaintiff cut off the four words above, presenting the case, requesting detailed investigation, and extended Wang Shizong lawyer defense. However, in this case, the plaintiff only submitted an account paper as evidence, and no strong evidence was presented. After the court's discussion, it was announced to be concluded and a date was set for the verdict.

1. Overview of Changes in Shanghai Industry and Commerce in September of the 25th Year (Continued)

2.

— Compiled by China Credit Bureau

(Twenty-ninth in the series of overviews of Shanghai industry and commerce)

(2) Guohua Textile Printing and Dyeing Factory is for sale. The factory was founded in July of the 24th year with a capital of 30,000 yuan in national currency, plus another 30,000 yuan in national currency, as a partnership. The major shareholder is Mr. Zhang Rongchu, but Mr. Zhang does not appear in person. Instead, Mr. Jing Songnian, another shareholder, serves as the manager. The factory site is on the old site of Tong Qiao Silk Factory, with two additional printing, dyeing, and mercerizing machines. The total equipment is worth over 100,000 yuan. It employs about 60 or 70 workers. It mainly provides printing and dyeing services for customers, and also dyes and sells gray fabrics itself. The maximum daily output can dye over 1,000 pieces of cloth. In the beginning, due to limited capital, the business was very small. Later, with the cooperation of Mr. Zhang, a giant in the dyeing industry, the business greatly improved. However, recently, due to sluggish business, the shareholders are not interested in continuing to operate, so they are selling the factory to the Central Printing and Dyeing Factory, it is said.

(3) Wei Chen Li Ji Silk Company Established. The company's manufacturing plant is located outside the East Gate of Jiaxing. Its predecessor was the Yujia Branch of Hangzhou Wei Cheng Company. The entire plant occupies more than 60 mu of land and is divided into three departments: silk, filature, and cocoon-making. The total construction and machinery equipment cost hundreds of thousands of yuan. In 1931, the factory and Hangzhou's headquarter closed down at the same time. The Zhejiang Provincial Department of Finance, since the company had previously mortgaged all of its real estate and machinery, the department guaranteed the issuance of company bonds. Since the company had already closed down, it was unable to fulfill its debt obligations as stipulated. Therefore, the department executed all of the mortgages and leased out the Hangzhou and Jiaxing factories separately. The Yujia Branch's silk department was leased by Wei Cheng Qing Ji. Later, the Department of Finance reached an agreement with the company's bondholders and preferential creditors to put the entire real estate and machinery of the Yujia Branch up for public auction at an estimated price. After three price reductions, the Shanghai Li Ji Company finally won the bid with the lowest price of 767,437 yuan. It also purchased the company's entire trademark rights for a price of 57,000 yuan, renaming it Wei Cheng Li Ji Silk Co., Ltd., specializing in silk. It is heard that the remaining filature and cocoon-making departments are still intended to be leased out. The founding meeting was held in Shanghai on the 20th of this month, and the head office is located at No. 16, Lane 149, Changsha Road in this city. The company was founded by Zheng Zanchen, Bao Mengwei, Zhu Ligeng, and others, and it has strong financial resources. Silk is inherently profitable and a new emerging industry, so the business has a good chance to succeed, it is said.

(4) Jinglun Silk Factory For Sale. The factory was established in 1930 and was founded solely by Mr. Zhou Baoliang. Mr. and Mrs. Zhou were previously workers at Wuhua Silk Factory. They lived frugally and saved a small amount of money, so they bought two looms. The total assets cost about 500 or 600 yuan. The couple worked hard and the business grew gradually. Later, they gradually expanded and purchased a total of nine motors and hired 18 workers and three or four apprentices. They specialized in weaving for landlords, and the livelihood was relatively stable. However, since the spring of last year, the silk industry has been declining due to poor market conditions and has been selling off at reduced prices. The factory was greatly affected. Since the autumn, silk prices have suddenly soared. The factory has a shortage of funds and is unable to advance money for weaving. Moreover, although silk prices have gradually increased, it is difficult to increase silk prices and market purchasing power has suddenly decreased. The situation is very difficult, and eventually it became heavily indebted and unable to maintain operations. Therefore, the creditors sold all of the factory's foundation, property, and machinery to Yuan Fengtai Ji Silk Factory for 600 yuan, it is said.

(5) Dasheng Machine Factory Liquidates and Sells. The factory was founded around 1925 and was operated solely by Mr. Xu Qingyun, with no fixed amount of capital. It employed 17 or 18 workers and specialized in manufacturing silk looms and water pumps. In the beginning, business was quite prosperous, especially for silk looms. However, since the January 28th Incident, the business of various silk factories has declined, and the demand for silk looms has also decreased accordingly. After 1934, business became even more sluggish. The factory then transformed to manufacture large and small water pumps. Because there were suitable droughts and disasters in various places at that time, the need for this machine was quite urgent, so it was able to rely on this to support and barely maintain operations. However, after the drought passed, the supply of the machine exceeded the demand, and business fell back into hardship. Extending to the 7th of this month, it finally announced liquidation and sale, it is said. (To be continued)

Hujiang Defeats Chizhi

Hujiang's strength this year is mediocre. They have lost to Tongji and Fudan. Chizhi is indeed an emerging strong team, coming with a sound and color, having defeated famous teams such as Fudan and Nanyang Tongji, so it was predicted that Hujiang was not their enemy, and the difference was very big. Unexpectedly, Hujiang consolidated its defense, preventing Chizhi from doing whatever they wanted, creating a stalemate situation that was difficult to resolve. On the other hand, Chizhi was flustered, and their formation was shattered. During the game, Hujiang led all the way, and Chizhi never took the lead. The excitement of the situation was even greater than the battle between Xintong and the Xin team.

Hujiang's victory, in summary, was due to the successful long shot by defender Lu Zhongyu, which earned a huge score. He had six successful shots, scoring a total of 13 points. Qian Jingyong also scored six goals and made three free throws, scoring 15 points. Feng Yulai's five goals were even more icing on the cake.

On the Chizhi side, although Liang Yunming scored the highest record of 23 points alone, center Chen Xuechong only scored eight points, and Shu Yinghai only scored three points, which was the biggest loss.

In the first half, except for two ties at 18 to 18 and 27 to 27, Hujiang often took the lead by one or two points, but it was only one or two points. Because of Qian Jingyong's shot, the score became 29 to 27, and Hujiang won by two points in the first half.

The situation afterwards was the same as in the previous game, struggling hard. In the last three or four minutes, Hujiang led by five points with a score of 46 to 41. After Liang Yunming and Chen Xuechong each scored a goal, they were only one point behind again. Lu Zhongyu got a free throw but missed, and suddenly Zhang Liangxiong's free throw made the final tie of 46 to 46. At this time, there was only one minute of precious time left. The two sides were caught in a bitter battle, and the emotions of the audience reached a boiling point. Chizhi attacked with all their strength, but Zhu Peisheng dribbled to the basket and got a long ball from the back, calmly put it into the most glorious two points, making Chizhi submit. The score of 48 to 46 meant that there was no ever-victorious army in the University Group. The progress of the subsequent games will be even more intriguing.

Education News

Teachers and Staff of Public Schools Exempted from Income Tax Deduction 154

Su Provincial Government Orders the Education Department to Inform

The Jiangsu Provincial Government instructed the Education Department, stating that in the past, considering that the salaries of teachers and staff in public schools in various counties of the province were meager, and in accordance with the provisions of the Provisional Income Tax Regulations that elementary school teachers and staff were exempt from taxation, the Ministry of Finance was consulted to exempt them from taxation. The Ministry of Finance replied, "Teachers and staff of public schools are serving compulsory social education, and their salaries are lower than those of elementary school teachers and staff. They can be exempted from withholding income tax on salaries and remuneration of civil servants in accordance with the provisions of Article 2, Category 2 of the Provisional Income Tax Regulations." It is hereby ordered to notify the relevant departments.

However, in the face of national crisis, our students must work hard, and once they have completed their studies, they can serve the country. Our "Support Suiyuan Movement" 160

— Gu Jingqun

Children! I think you have all seen the news in the newspapers recently about the rampant bandits and traitors invading our borders and attacking Suiyuan, and the news of them opening fire with the garrison! After seeing this, will we once think about the advantages and disadvantages of it? We must know that Suiyuan is the first line of defense for our country, and the gain or loss of Suiyuan is a key to the life and death of our Republic of China, so we must pay close attention to it and not ignore it. We have also seen the soldiers at the front of Suiyuan, who are full of boiling blood, bravely fighting in the freezing weather to defend the country's territory, and resolutely not losing an inch of land to the enemy. This spirit is worthy of our admiration.

Now all sectors of Shanghai are enthusiastically donating money and sending it to Suiyuan to provide material assistance to comfort our loyal and brave soldiers who are seeking survival for the country and the nation! Children! We are also part of the citizens of the Republic of China, and we must also fulfill our national duty. We must save money from various expenses such as candy, toys, and snacks, and donate it to the Suiyuan soldiers who are serving the country. Although the money saved by one person is very limited, I believe that if we calculate the money saved by children all over the country, there will definitely be a huge sum of money, enough to give the Suiyuan soldiers great material assistance. Therefore, I hope that children all over the country will unite and contribute to the soldiers at the front.

Letter to Mother 164

— Qian Zhongzheng

Mother:

I reluctantly suppressed my infinite sorrow and passion to write this farewell letter to you.

I am now on the front lines of the battlefield. I have no other thoughts. In my mind, there is only the thought of sacrificing for the country. I dare not even think of you. If I think of your kindness and your greatness, I am afraid it will reduce my spirit to kill the enemy. Although the people who die for the country are very regrettable, they are sacrificing for justice and fairness, so it is not a waste to die.

I have forgotten what you said to me at the farewell. All I remember is: "I hope you die on the battlefield, don't die at home, and I don't want to see you before the enemy soldiers are driven back." I can't remember the other words. The words I remember are those that can make me strive forward bravely, repel the enemy, and prepare to see you, my great and kind mother, and receive your kiss and embrace. I want to receive your kiss and embrace immediately, so I have to repel this enemy immediately.

Mother! I hope you become the greatest patriotic mother in China, and I hope other people's mothers are like you too. Mother! You don't have to be sad. Mr. Wen Tianxiang once said, "Who has not died since ancient times, but let my loyal heart shine in history!" It's just a matter of dying sooner or later. You don't have to think that you will never see your lively and lovely son again. As Mr. Lin Juemin said, "Living in today's era, thieves can die, corrupt officials who abuse the people can die, and living in today's China, there is no place where one cannot die. It is better to die for the sake of fighting for national survival!"

Mother! Don't be sad that you don't have a son. I didn't believe in ghosts originally, but now I really hope there are ghosts after death. I hope this is reliable, so that you can still see your lively son, and you won't be sad!

Now the bugle has sounded, and we are about to proceed. Goodbye! Kind mother! Finally, I have to call out again: "Long live the Republic of China! Long live the Republic of China!"

A Necessary Understanding of Suiyuan 168

— Ji

As Suiyuan is being invaded by bandits, puppet regimes, and enemies, I believe that children should have at least the following knowledge of Suiyuan: Suiyuan, together with Rehe and Chahar, is known as Inner Mongolia. It was designated as a special region in the third year of the Republic of China (1914) and reorganized as a province in September of the seventeenth year (1928). It governs seventeen counties, two administrative bureaus, and two leagues (thirteen banners, five gentry and one general administrator). The provincial capital is Guisui.

The total area of Suiyuan is 304,058 square kilometers. The total population is 1,805,799.

Suiyuan's products: Animals are mostly oxen, horses, sheep, mules, and camels, with leather and wool being the main exports. Plants are mostly grains, timber, and medicinal materials. Minerals are mostly coal and iron, with silver, aluminum, oil, salt, and soda also available. Handicrafts are mostly woolen and leather products and felt carpets.

Suiyuan transportation: The railway includes the Fenggui section and the Suibao section of the Ping-Sui Railway. The two sections are more than 739 li long in total. There are 602 kilometers of completed highways. Telecommunications: Wired telegraph, wireless telegraph, long-distance telephone, etc. are all available. There are more than 60 post offices. Aviation: Airports are located in Guisui and Baotou.

As the saying goes: "Of all the rivers in the world, the Yellow River is the richest." The Yellow River's backset is entirely within Suiyuan. These areas have fertile land and vast fields, making them ideal for cultivation.

Children! The enemies have coveted these resources for a long time. If we do not rise up to defend our territory and preserve our resources, the consequences will be unimaginable!

Suiyuan and Chairman Fu 169

— (Zhu Guang)

Children, the "Sui" in Suiyuan means stability, and "Yuan" means far and near. Combining them, it means being stable and far away. But those thieves were unlucky and ran into a nail, but they ran into our teacher "Fu". He is a chairman who is "capable" and doesn't give way, and sees "righteousness" and acts bravely. Therefore, when the thieves came to spy on him, he decided to give them a head-on blow, which was also expected.

— Xian Weisheng

Children, the news of the "bandit and puppet invasion of Suiyuan" must have been seen in the newspapers by everyone. If it weren't for Chairman Fu Zuoyi's "death pledge" to resist the war and defend the country, the consequences would have been unimaginable!

However, resisting the enemy is not just empty talk. There must be sufficient "strength" and a steady stream of supplies to be sustained.

I remember that during the "September 18th Incident" when General Ma Zhanshan resisted the enemy, you did save a lot of candy money to donate to the Northeast Volunteer Army as military pay. To this day, people still often mention this and praise your good deeds. For the present plan, needless to say, it is "one more time". Save the candy money as usual and donate it to the "soldiers on the front lines", which is easier. Fortunately, candy is just a snack, so you can eat less of it. If one person donates ten cents, one hundred people will make ten yuan, and ten thousand people will make one thousand yuan. That amount is really not small!

Children! Please everyone, "one more time"!

Filial Piety (7) 172

— Hai

Finally, a solution came to mind. One of the coachmen said, "Let's take turns lending him our leather coats, or just let him wear it all the way, and we'll switch every mile," he suggested, and everyone agreed. Immediately, one of the coachmen took off his sheepskin coat and put it on Boskoffy carefully, while he wrapped himself in the cargo cloth, curled up his feet underneath him, and sang even louder. Every time they saw a milestone, they would have to take off the sheepskin coat and have a happy chat while changing clothes. Along the way, Boskoffy prayed silently that they would not harm their health because of this.

When they arrived at the inn in Yekaterinburg, the hostess of the inn told her about several philanthropists in the town, and especially praised Madam Millin, saying that she was charitable and everyone knew it. She asked Boskoffy to see this madam tomorrow to discuss how to proceed. It just so happened that the next day was Sunday, so Boskoffy hurried to church. Her devout prayer and the tattered travel clothes she wore attracted people's attention. As she walked out of the church, a lady asked her name. Boskoffy told her the name and asked her to point out where Madam Millin lived, and said that the madam's charity was well known. The lady said to her, "I'm afraid Madam Millin's charity is a bit too much; you might as well come with me and let me take care of you."

Boskoffy didn't like to hear this kind of disparaging remark about Madam Millin, so the lady quickly pointed out where Madam Millin lived, and told her that if she was refused, she could go to her. Boskoffy didn't answer and walked to Madam Millin's door to ask the servants if the madam was home. The servants looked at their mistress in surprise. It turned out that the lady who was talking to her was Madam Millin herself.

This charitable madam left her at home and treated her as a guest. She stayed there for a whole winter and tried her best to heal the frostbite she had suffered in the wind and snow that night. At the same time, she gave Boskoffy a general education. Since her father was exiled to Siberia, Boskoffy had almost forgotten how to read and write. Now she began to read, draw, and write again. Every time she talked about Madam Millin's charity, she couldn't help but shed tears of gratitude. But while she was living comfortably, she felt even more uncomfortable when she thought of her parents suffering in the snow and ice. However, Madam Millin refused to let her leave Yekaterinburg until the spring of the following year, when she bought her a seat on a flat-bottomed boat on the Kama River and entrusted the people on the boat to take good care of her. This person was carrying a boatload of iron and salt to Nizhny Novgorod.

Unfortunately, this person suddenly fell ill and had to stay in a small village on the Kama River. So Boskoffy set off alone again without anyone to look after her.

Current Affairs Research

After the Formation of the German-Italian-Japanese Bloc 173

— Zhong He

Recently, there have been two issues of international concern that have shocked the world, namely the successive establishment of the German-Japanese and Italian-Japanese agreements. The establishment of these two agreements not only shows that the relationship between Western aggressors and Japan is closer, but also shows that the three countries of Germany, Italy, and Japan have formed a bloc. Although Italy has not yet joined the German-Japanese agreement, and Germany has no direct relationship with the Italian-Japanese agreement, and the three countries of Italy, Germany, and Japan have not yet openly signed a treaty of alliance, judging from the national conditions of these three countries and their foreign policies, judging from the nature of the two agreements they recently established, they are standing on the same front in some respects. The formation of this bloc's front is certainly not for so-called "self-defense," because Germany, Italy, and Japan are all so-called powerful countries. Their territories have never been plundered, and their internal affairs have not been interfered with. There is no basis for raising the so-called "self-defense" issue. As for jointly defending against the development of any ideology, that is a matter of domestic thought and does not require any agreement to deal with it. If we are not deceived by those international diplomatic articles, then we can point out that the actual intention of Germany and Japan and Italy and Japan in establishing agreements is to mutually recognize "faits accomplis," jointly defend the lands they have seized, and work together to invade weak nations and attack world peace. We see that Article 1 of the German-Japanese agreement does not already hint that they want to force countries threatened by some force to surrender to them? Does not Article 3 of the attached protocol stipulate that they should establish a standing committee to deal with everything? What is the meaning of these? All those who love peace and respect their own country's sovereignty fully understand this. If we say that because of the establishment of the Italian-Japanese agreement, Japan thereby recognizes Italy's annexation of Abyssinia, then the meaning is even clearer; no one can say that it is for so-called "self-defense" and "peace."

Japan's recent actions in the Far East have been surprising enough; now that it has the assistance of the two Western countries, Italy and Germany, it is certainly "like a tiger with wings," and it will continue to make more serious demonstrations. Hitler and Mussolini are both world-renowned "eccentrics" and the greatest enemies of peace. In the past, they have fired many cannons, torn up many international treaties, and insulted and trampled on the weak nations and oppressed people of the world, and even general liberals. Now that they have Japan in the East to support them, it will certainly prompt them to attack the peace forces of the world even more. Originally, "birds of a feather flock together," and it is not surprising that the three countries of Germany, Italy, and Japan form a bloc, but from then on, the security of Europe and the Pacific, the peace of the world, and the fate of weak nations and the generally oppressed will be threatened even more powerfully; in the past, their acts of aggression were individual, but now they have become more organized and planned collective actions.

Taking the countries of the world as a whole, the most threatened by the formation of the German-Italian-Japanese bloc is, of course, the Soviet Union, because the Soviet Union's social system is fundamentally different from theirs, and the Soviet Union's peaceful diplomacy is also in contradiction with their aggressive actions, and they are opposed to each other in all respects. In addition to the Soviet Union, the major powers such as Britain, the United States, and France are also under their serious threat. As for weak nations such as China, they have even more keenly felt the increase in the forces of aggression. Let's take Britain first.

After the German-Japanese agreement was announced, political circles in London expressed alarm and suspicion. At the same time, the "Standard Evening News" also reported that the German-Japanese agreement was attached with secret conditions, the main points of which were: "(1) The Dutch East Indies shall be divided into spheres of influence for Germany and Japan, and (2) Resolve the issue of Germany's pre-war possessions in the Pacific Islands." In other words, Borneo and Celebes in the Dutch East Indies are to be used as Japan's sphere of influence, while Sumatra and Java are to be used as Germany's sphere of influence; at the same time, Germany declares that it will abandon all rights to the Mariana, Caroline, and Marshall Islands (currently under Japanese mandate) that it owned in the Pacific before the war. If this is true, then Japan's southward advance will be even more convenient, and thus Britain's rights in Southeast Asia, and even in India and Burma, and in the entire Pacific will be threatened even more. Even if these private conditions are completely "rumors," because of the assistance of Germany and Italy, Japan's power in China (the country) and in the Pacific will also expand significantly, and Britain's security in the East will also be very problematic. At the same time, Britain is currently arguing with Italy in the Mediterranean, while Tokyo and Rome are staging a duet: Italy is befriending Japan, and Japan has also recognized Abyssinia as Italian territory, which is also something that Britain is not happy about; although Mussolini is unwilling to join the German-Japanese agreement in order to establish a Mediterranean "gentleman's agreement" with Britain, in London's view, the two enemies in the East and West are gathering together and getting hot, which is always unfavorable to it. Therefore, both the German-Japanese and Italian-Japanese agreements are opposed by London; this can be seen not only in the media, but also in the statements of government officials. However, Hitler stubbornly refused to understand, and he even ordered the German ambassador to Britain to inquire whether Baldwin could join the German-Japanese Anti-Comintern Pact, which resulted in a hard snub. The cunning old fox Baldwin actually flatly refused to consider the question he raised.

Although the United States is farther away from the Far East and has repeatedly stated that it is unwilling to interfere in European affairs, the large-scale gathering of aggressive forces and the growth of Japanese power in the Pacific are also things that Washington is unwilling to hear. Therefore, after the news of the establishment of the German-Japanese and Italian-Japanese agreements was released, although the United States expressed a consistent "neutral attitude," it still paid close attention to the new situation of the German-Italian-Japanese bloc and deeply felt the great threat to world peace; as for the American media, it expressed its opposition even more clearly.

France is also greatly threatened by the German-Italian-Japanese group. In recent years, Hitler's risky actions to undermine international treaties have long made France feel its own security problems; for this reason, Paris has signed a treaty with the Soviet Union, which promotes a policy of peace, and is actively wooing Britain to prevent the development of aggressive forces. At that time, Hitler also expressed great indignation, saying that the peaceful group was dangerous to peace, and used this pretext to tear up international treaties again and erect cannons on the banks of the Rhine River aimed at Paris. But what about now? Hitler himself has also formed a bloc with Italy and Japan, preparing to attack the Soviet Union, the signatory of the Franco-Soviet agreement, in the East, threatening peace in the Pacific, and directly threatening France's security in the West. Now, Hitler and Mussolini have openly divided Central Europe into their spheres of influence, treating Czechoslovakia and Austria as targets of German aggression, and counting Hungary and Yugoslavia as areas of Italian aggression. This not only makes the small countries of Central Europe feel their own survival problems, but France also has to feel greatly uneasy, because the small countries of Central Europe are France's barrier. Therefore, after the establishment of the German-Italian-Japanese group, the French authorities immediately took "preventive measures" to ensure the security of Europe; and the Paris newspapers unanimously opposed it, and called on the French people to rise up to defend world peace.

Based on the above analysis, we can see that on the one hand, there is a large-scale gathering of aggressive forces, threatening world peace and the security of all countries, and on the other hand, there is the opposition and defense of many countries in the world to aggressionism. In today's world, it is "if the devil is one foot tall, the way is also one foot tall." As the forces that undermine peace develop, the forces that defend peace are also developing; otherwise, the cruel god of war would have already descended on the world. Look, regarding the gathering of aggressive forces, France, the Soviet Union, and China have expressed their firm opposition, and Britain and the United States have also expressed that they will not support them. Even Poland and Austria, which have always followed behind Hitler and Mussolini, are unwilling to join their group. These are all concrete answers to the aggressors. Of course, we cannot say that world peace has been guaranteed, and that the liberation of weak nations has had more favorable conditions. On the contrary, due to the establishment of the aggressive group, the war crisis is even more imminent, and the liberation of weak nations has increased some difficulties, but the aggressive forces want to win, I am afraid that it is just an illusion.

Features

A Sketch of Aid-Sui Movements in Various Circles of This City 174

— Fei Hong

"Aid Sui!" This clamor, like the cannons of "January 28th," shook everyone's eardrums in Shanghai. At the same time, there was a widespread resonance across the country, making Shanghai, which had been silent for a very long time, seem to hold up countless torches in the still night. The author, unable to march to northern Henan and personally witness the scenes of beacon fires and the courageous fight against the enemy to save the country, felt that the light of these torches already raised in this city was no less than the beacon fires on the front lines.

"Those with money, give money!" Under this call, we saw many well-dressed people gathering in their offices, writing rooms, and clubs, three or five, eight or ten at a time, to discuss. Some responded to the "One-Day Movement," declaring to the accountant that they were willing to donate a full day's salary each month, contributing their bit to the cause and sending it to aid Sui. This included public and clerical staff, business managers and employees, and so on. After these discussions, they would prepare a large sheet of white paper with the following words written on it:

"The national Aid Sui movement should be unified! We are also part of the Chinese nation, and we dare not lag behind others in loving our country. Therefore, after discussions among several people, we will donate one day's income from each person's monthly salary. Every little helps, and we will send it to the front lines. Please sign your names!"

Below this, we could see many names. Some were written with ink brushes, some with fountain pens, and some with pencils. But all were signed very quickly and smoothly, expressing a willing attitude on the surface of the words.

I left the well-dressed people and went out into the streets. Although the north wind was howling and the cold air was biting, the Boy Scouts, who were not seeking fame or profit and braving the cold wind, were already active in the streets, urging people to donate. Several Girl Scouts walked up to me, their hands already frozen purple. Their voices were trembling, and their bodies were shivering. They said in unison:

"Sir! The weather is very cold today, isn't it? The soldiers in northern Sui, who are in ice and snow ten times colder than Shanghai, need our help even more!"

The short sentences stung my heart. I fumbled in my warm inner pocket for a small banknote and handed it to them with shame. Accidentally touching an ice-cold palm made me feel an unusual excitement!

In other places, I saw some Boy Scouts walking past one or two poorly dressed laborers. They did not ask them for money. But the two laborers each voluntarily took out a dozen copper coins and gave them to them, saying:

"This is a good thing! Thank you for your hard work. I'll donate a little too!"

This was in the so-called factory area. I visited a familiar factory. It was not possible to move freely here, but because I had a good relationship with the manager and administrators, once I entered the door, I could run around as I pleased. In a workshop where people were working hard and taking breaks to chat, I saw most of the workers looking pale and malnourished. One talkative person was broadcasting news:

"Fighting the bandit army is just like fighting ××, isn't it? It's really great! Everyone is donating money again like during 'January 28th'! There was a place where prisoners even went hungry for a day and used that as a donation!"

"Let's donate some too!" Several people said in unison.

"The labor union has already discussed a plan!" someone reminded.

"Let them deduct a little from our wages or savings!"

"Deduct from savings! We might as well ask them to deduct a good amount!"

"The more people there are, the better it will look! It will always amount to hundreds and thousands!"

"Ha! Ha! Ha!" A burst of self-comforting laughter.

At this time, I also joined in with a wry smile, and then I went elsewhere.

This was a certain girls' middle school that first initiated the donation of silk cotton vests. I followed a photographer in. The place where they were making cotton clothes was the self-study classroom. The sound of scissors and whispers echoed each other. Suddenly, when we walked in, we heard them humming the graduation song of "Tao Li Jie" and the "March of the Volunteers":

"Compatriots, rise up and take on the responsibility of the rise and fall of the world!"

"People who do not want to be slaves! Rise up! Advance in the face of the enemy's artillery fire!"

The heavy air solidified everyone's spirit into serious work. Everyone was burying themselves in sewing. On a wooden table that resembled a large dining table, several finished silk cotton vests had already been piled up. They felt very soft to the touch. The outer fabric was patriotic cloth, and the lining was plain cloth, roughly two feet four or five inches long. These were prepared to be worn inside military uniforms and tucked into military trousers. It was imagined that they must be warm and practical.

"The maiden's hand sews the thread, the warrior wears the clothes!"

They were truly practicing: "Peace, struggle, save China!"

Wherever you go to inquire: whether it is gentle,激烈的, excited, calm... everyone is doing their best, donating enthusiastically, and finding ways to raise funds. The newspapers show news of the aid Sui groups every day; the notice boards of factories and shops are posted with news of the aid Sui activities; the school's wall newspaper is brilliant with large characters. Statements from the literary world donating manuscript fees for paintings and calligraphy; student composition topics; one of the reasons for store sales; film merchants, dance halls, taverns, and restaurants are all encouraging and calling for this!

It is as if Shanghai, with its paper drunkeness and gold-digging, has put on a gas mask of national salvation movement! Ah, the great and enthusiastic aid Sui movement!

Philosophy Lecture

The Problem of the Elimination of Philosophy 176

— Shi Ji

"Philosophy not only explains the world, but also changes the world." Someone also said, "Once a new philosophy grasps the masses, it becomes the spiritual weapon of the masses." From this point of view, philosophy is very important now. Moreover, philosophy has a history of thousands of years, and now, not only has it not found its demise, but it has unfolded a brand-new world. From the past and present status of philosophy, it seems that it will not be eliminated in the near future.

But there are also people there advocating the theory of the elimination of philosophy. Some oppose philosophy from the standpoint of natural scientists. This point has already been discussed. Natural researchers always believe that as long as they despise philosophy and scold philosophy, they can be liberated from the constant presence of philosophy. But they do not think, and cannot move forward even one step. And for this thinking, theoretical provisions are necessary." So philosophy is still necessary. There are also some philosophers who abolish philosophy from their own standpoint. In Soviet Russia, there are Stepanov et al. In China, this issue is also raging fiercely. Therefore, we have the necessity to bring it up for discussion.

Since some people advocate the theory of the elimination of philosophy, there will naturally be many people who oppose this view, saying that philosophy will not be eliminated. Those who oppose philosophy from the standpoint of natural scientists, their reasons are completely mechanical and naive materialist views, which have already been refuted, and there is no need to repeat them here. As for those who advocate the elimination of philosophy from the standpoint of philosophers, the reasons they hold and the reasons held by those who refute them must be introduced. Here we can divide it into two aspects. The first point is theoretical, and the second point is textual. Of course, their theoretical basis also stems from the documents they understand, but in addition to the documents they cite, they always have their own logic. So it can be roughly divided into two aspects. Of course, both factions claim to be standing on the standpoint of new philosophy, and the documents on which they are based are also common.

We will now first examine the textual aspect:

The documents on which those who advocate the elimination of philosophy are based are as follows: "Philosophy generally ends with Hegel, on the one hand because he summarized the entire development on a large scale into his system, and on the other hand he, even unconsciously, actually pointed out to us the true path to reach the positiveness of the world outside the labyrinth of the system" (Engels, Anti-Dühring). "Modern materialism is not simply a reappearance of old materialism, but adds the entire ideological content of two thousand years of philosophy, natural science, and the development of two thousand years of history itself to the solid foundation of materialism. Generally speaking, this is no longer philosophy, but a pure worldview, which should not find its proof on some special branch of science, but on real science, and express its function. In this way, philosophy is "sublated," formally overcome, but retained in actual content" (Ibid.).

Based on the above grounds, those who advocate the elimination of philosophy conclude that this is the "end of philosophy."

On the other hand, those who oppose him cited many documents: "After understanding the results of the philosophical development of the past fifteen hundred years, natural science, on the one hand, can get rid of the special natural philosophy that is separate from it and above it, and on the other hand, can get rid of its own narrow way of thinking transmitted from English experience" (Anti-Dühring). "After philosophy is driven out of the natural world and history, only one area remains for it to place itself. This area is pure thought: the theory of studying the laws of thought - logic and dialectics" (Religion, Philosophy, and Socialism). "When natural science and historical science adopt dialectics in them, all the waste of philosophy - except for the theory of pure thought - begins to become superfluous and disappears into empirical science" (Collected Letters, Volume 4).

Based on the above, the opponents concluded that the philosophy eliminated by Engels was natural philosophy and historical philosophy, the old philosophy that was independent of science and above science, and that "logic and dialectics" were still not eliminated.

This is the textual argument between the two factions.

Let us look at the reasons held by the two from a theoretical point of view:

Those who advocate the elimination of philosophy believe that everything is in motion and change, everything has its birth, development, and death, so philosophy also has its death and elimination. Ever since philosophy became independent from religion, it denied religion; now that science is independent from philosophy, science will deny philosophy, and philosophy will be eliminated.

The opponents say: As science develops, philosophy will naturally be negated, but what is negated is the old philosophy in philosophy, such as natural philosophy and historical philosophy, not all of philosophy, including dialectical materialism - "logic and dialectics." So philosophy has not been eliminated. Moreover, dialectics is the general law of motion of nature, society, and thought, while science is the study of the laws of parts of the universe, so science still needs philosophy to guide and summarize it, and science cannot replace philosophy.

At the same time, according to the meaning of those who advocate the elimination of philosophy, the philosophy that he eliminates, the philosophy that he believes should eliminate itself, is only "old philosophy," "philosophical philosophy," while the dialectical materialism of new philosophy - "scientific philosophy" - is not in the list of elimination.

Then aren't the claims of these two factions going to reach the same conclusion in the end? Both say that the philosophy that is eliminated is old philosophy, idealistic philosophy, natural philosophy, historical philosophy, or "philosophical philosophy," while "scientific philosophy" is not eliminated, and no one attempts to, and no one can, eliminate it. In this way, the argument between these two seems to be just an argument over names, and it is only an argument over the scope of the meaning of the term philosophy. According to the former, the elimination of old philosophy is regarded as the elimination of the entire philosophy, hence the theory of the elimination of philosophy: in the latter, it is necessary to say separately that the elimination of old philosophy is not the elimination of the entire philosophy. This can be fully seen in the recent arguments between the two factions. That is, according to the meaning of nouns. In the theory of philosophical extinction, dialectical materialism is no longer philosophy, but has really become the theory of science. As a result, the term philosophy has generally lost its meaning of existence, and only science exists. On the other hand, opponents believe that the dialectical materialism is not science, but although it is a "scientific" philosophy, it is still philosophy, but it is different from "unscientific" philosophy. And now science still needs this new philosophy, which is not separate from science and does not stand above science, to guide it. So philosophy still exists.

In order to eliminate philosophy, those who advocate the elimination of philosophy have established a science of thinking, believing that the only territory that philosophy can retain - pure thought - can also be the field of science. In this way, philosophy has no place to stand. But at the same time, some people oppose the establishment of a science of thinking, and some people believe that science is the study of general laws of movement, so whether the science of thinking can be established has nothing to do with whether philosophy will be eliminated.

From the above, the question of whether philosophy is eliminated can be said to be an unresolved question. We hope that all philosophy researchers will enthusiastically participate in this debate and demonstrate from the textual and theoretical perspectives. At the same time, we also hope that the question of the establishment of a science of thinking, and the question of whether the establishment of a science of thinking and philosophy will be eliminated, will be studied together.

Also, in the Chinese philosophical community, the question of whether idealism and materialism can be synthesized is now also very fierce. What we want to say here is that this question is also related to the question of philosophical elimination. Because those who advocate that the two can be synthesized say that the history of philosophy is the reason why philosophy can become philosophy, because there is the contradiction and struggle between idealism and materialism, and philosophy is the product of this contradiction and opposition. If these two opposing things are unified, then the debate will disappear, and thus philosophy will also disappear. But whether these two can be unified, and whether the unification of these two will eliminate philosophy, is still a question to be studied. This also needs to be merged into the previous item for discussion.

Life

Nurse Miss 177

— Ms. Rong

The first day of work gave me the impression that, apart from the suffocating smell of medicine, it surprisingly felt no different from the factory life two years ago. If I had to find its difference, it would only be the difference in address. Before, when working, people would call my name, but now, as a nurse, I have been changed to "Miss." The so-called Miss is just a little foreign. If it is really a lady from a boudoir, who would be willing to do those dirty things for patients, even the lowest-level things have to be done! From 7:00 a.m. to 7:00 p.m., we have no free time to rest during these twelve hours. For example, I work in the examination room. Just the routine things I have to do every day, from wiping medicine bottles, disinfecting, preparing the medicine to be used every day, and sorting out the examination room and medical records, take up an hour or two. Often, by 8:00 a.m., patients have come to see the doctor, and our work is not fully prepared. So we have to use the nurse's skill of lying to people, and lie to the patients, "Please wait a moment, the doctor will come soon." In fact, the doctor only comes when we ask him to come. Sometimes our work takes a long time to finish, and we are afraid that the patients will be impatient and anxious, so we have to use the same tone to coax the patients again. When we have finished this part of our work, the clinic is always full of patients. At this time, we are happy to use nice words to tell the patients, "What, the doctor hasn't come yet? Let me call him." The patient usually replies "Thank you!" to express thanks.

The doctor is called, and we have to do the work of the doctor's assistant. We pay attention at all times, and send up whatever the doctor needs, and we have to be quick and agile. In the summer, if the doctor's hands are disinfected, we have to wipe the sweat from his face for him. I have also done this work under the guidance of senior students. In the first few days, I felt that this work was too vulgar. It was as if we were female servants who were called to do rough work by the hospital in a brothel. In fact, we are not even as good as them. They still have three or four yuan in wages every month, but we have to give money to the hospital. Of course, the hospital also says it sounds nice: free learning, only charge for food. But what do we really learn? Originally, there is one hour a day to read books, but in fact, we only have one or two hours of classes a week at most.

One day, my work was particularly busy, and I hardly rested all day, and the doctor was very greedy for playing, and when he had a little free time, he disappeared. One wanted to see the doctor, and the other wanted to see the doctor, so we looked for the doctor everywhere. It was tiring enough to find him, let alone do things! When I returned to the dormitory and talked to my classmates about this, my classmate Ms. Li heard and said, "It's considered that you are doing the most pleasant job in the ENT department, and there are no extremely dirty patients. It's the hardest for me to do in the ward. I didn't rest at all last night, all of them were seriously ill. This place wasn't busy, and then the doorbell rang again. Patient No. 20 is the worst, ringing the doorbell for no reason. When I went, he said: He was very lonely and wanted us to relieve his boredom. This kind of person simply regards our nurses as a pastime. It's really irritating - and there are the lying-in woman of No. 30 and the syphilis patient of No. 16, which are extremely annoying, ringing the doorbell all the time, and it's so troublesome to go, wanting this and that, and being busy endlessly. That syphilis patient is already in his forties, and always wants to tell us jokes. If we don't perfunctorily him, then he will tell the head nurse, saying that a certain nurse is not good, and so on. So we will inevitably be given a demerit. Gu and Wang are examples, so we have to perfunctorily him a few words. But his affairs are really troublesome enough, what: 'Today's medicine is not comfortable, can you change it for me?' I often have to change it for him, but it's really embarrassing to apply medicine for him."

"You haven't done surgery yet." Zhao Xiangzhen said to me, "Those patients with rotten heads and feet are dirty and smelly, but we have to wash the pus from these patients. Sometimes we are a little careless, and we touch our faces with our unsterilized hands after washing the rotten things, and we may get the same sores."
